### File: app.py
```
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify, render_template
from flask_cors import CORS
from extractors import extract_from_pdf, extract_from_docx, extract_from_url
from quiz_generator import generate_quiz

app = Flask(__name__)
CORS(app)

ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS = {"pdf", "docx"}


def allowed_file(filename: str) -> bool:
    return "." in filename and filename.rsplit(".", 1)[1].lower() in ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS


@app.route("/")
def index():
    return render_template("index.html")


@app.route("/api/extract", methods=["POST"])
def extract():
    """Extract text from uploaded file or URL."""
    text = ""

    if "file" in request.files:
        file = request.files["file"]
        if not allowed_file(file.filename):
            return jsonify({"error": "Only PDF and DOCX files are supported."}), 400
        ext = file.filename.rsplit(".", 1)[1].lower()
        text = extract_from_pdf(file) if ext == "pdf" else extract_from_docx(file)

    elif request.json and request.json.get("url"):
        try:
            text = extract_from_url(request.json["url"])
        except Exception as e:
            return jsonify({"error": f"URL extraction failed: {str(e)}"}), 400
    else:
        return jsonify({"error": "Provide a file or URL."}), 400

    if not text.strip():
        return jsonify({"error": "No text could be extracted."}), 400

    return jsonify({"text": text[:8000], "char_count": len(text)})


@app.route("/api/generate", methods=["POST"])
def generate():
    """Generate quiz from extracted text."""
    data = request.json
    required = ["text", "mode", "difficulty"]
    if not all(k in data for k in required):
        return jsonify({"error": f"Missing fields: {required}"}), 400

    try:
        result = generate_quiz(
            text=data["text"],
            mode=data["mode"],           # mcq | flashcard | both
            difficulty=data["difficulty"],  # easy | medium | hard
            topic_filter=data.get("topic_filter", ""),
            count=int(data.get("count", 5)),
        )
        return jsonify(result)
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({"error": str(e)}), 500


if __name__ == "__main__":
    app.run(debug=True)
```

### File: extractors.py
```
import fitz  # PyMuPDF
import docx
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup


def extract_from_pdf(file) -> str:
    doc = fitz.open(stream=file.read(), filetype="pdf")
    return "\n".join(page.get_text() for page in doc)


def extract_from_docx(file) -> str:
    document = docx.Document(file)
    return "\n".join(p.text for p in document.paragraphs if p.text.strip())


def extract_from_url(url: str) -> str:
    """Basic extraction — caller can replace clean_text logic later."""
    response = requests.get(url, timeout=10, headers={"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"})
    response.raise_for_status()
    soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, "html.parser")

    # Remove noise tags
    for tag in soup(["script", "style", "nav", "footer", "header", "aside"]):
        tag.decompose()

    # TODO: plug in your custom cleaning code here
    raw_text = soup.get_text(separator="\n")
    lines = [line.strip() for line in raw_text.splitlines() if line.strip()]
    return "\n".join(lines)
```

### File: quiz_generator.py
```
import json
import os
from openai import OpenAI
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()
client = OpenAI(
    api_key=os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY"),
    base_url="https://api.groq.com/openai/v1"
)

DIFFICULTY_HINTS = {
    "easy": "Use simple language. Focus on basic definitions and facts.",
    "medium": "Include conceptual understanding and application-based questions.",
    "hard": "Include analysis, inference, and multi-step reasoning questions.",
}


def _chat(messages: list, model="llama-3.1-8b-instant") -> str:
    response = client.chat.completions.create(model=model, messages=messages)
    return response.choices[0].message.content.strip()


# ── Chain Step 1: Extract key topics from raw text ──────────────────────────
def extract_topics(text: str, topic_filter: str = None) -> str:
    prompt = f"Extract the main educational topics from the following text as a concise bullet list."
    if topic_filter:
        prompt += f" Focus only on topics related to: {topic_filter}."
    prompt += f"\n\nText:\n{text[:6000]}"

    return _chat([
        {"role": "system", "content": "You are an expert educator and content analyst."},
        {"role": "user", "content": prompt},
    ])


# ── Chain Step 2: Generate MCQs from topics + text ──────────────────────────
def generate_mcqs(text: str, topics: str, difficulty: str, count: int = 5) -> list:
    hint = DIFFICULTY_HINTS.get(difficulty, DIFFICULTY_HINTS["medium"])
    prompt = f"""You are a quiz generator. Based on the topics and source text below, generate {count} multiple-choice questions.

Difficulty: {difficulty.upper()} — {hint}

Topics:
{topics}

Source Text (excerpt):
{text[:5000]}

Return ONLY a JSON array in this exact format:
[
  {{
    "question": "...",
    "options": {{"A": "...", "B": "...", "C": "...", "D": "..."}},
    "answer": "A",
    "explanation": "..."
  }}
]"""

    raw = _chat([
        {"role": "system", "content": "You are a precise quiz generator. Output only valid JSON."},
        {"role": "user", "content": prompt},
    ])
    return _parse_json(raw)


# ── Chain Step 3: Generate Flashcards ───────────────────────────────────────
def generate_flashcards(text: str, topics: str, difficulty: str, count: int = 5) -> list:
    hint = DIFFICULTY_HINTS.get(difficulty, DIFFICULTY_HINTS["medium"])
    prompt = f"""Generate {count} flashcards from the topics and text below.

Difficulty: {difficulty.upper()} — {hint}

Topics:
{topics}

Source Text (excerpt):
{text[:5000]}

Return ONLY a JSON array:
[
  {{
    "front": "Question or term",
    "back": "Answer or definition"
  }}
]"""

    raw = _chat([
        {"role": "system", "content": "You are a flashcard creator. Output only valid JSON."},
        {"role": "user", "content": prompt},
    ])
    return _parse_json(raw)


# ── Output Parser ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
def _parse_json(raw: str) -> list:
    """Strip markdown fences and parse JSON safely."""
    cleaned = raw.strip()
    if cle
```

### File: README.md
```
# 🧠 QuizBuddy — AI Study Buddy

QuizBuddy is an AI-powered study assistant that transforms your study material into interactive quizzes and flashcards instantly. Simply upload a PDF, Word document, or paste a URL — QuizBuddy extracts the content, detects key topics using prompt chaining, and generates MCQs or flashcards tailored to your chosen difficulty level. It's built to make revision faster, smarter, and more engaging.

## 🛠 Tech Stack

| Layer | Technology |
|---|---|
| Backend | Python, Flask, Flask-CORS |
| AI / LLM | Groq API (`llama-3.1-8b-instant`) via OpenAI-compatible SDK |
| PDF Extraction | PyMuPDF (fitz) |
| DOCX Extraction | python-docx |
| URL Extraction | Requests + BeautifulSoup4 |
| Frontend | HTML, CSS, Vanilla JavaScript |
| Config | python-dotenv |

## 📁 Project Structure

```
QuizBuddy/
├── app.py              # Flask server & API routes
├── extractors.py       # PDF, DOCX, URL text extraction
├── quiz_generator.py   # Prompt chaining + output parsing
├── requirements.txt    # Python dependencies
├── .env                # API key (not pushed to GitHub)
├── assets/             # Screenshots & demo
├── static/
│   ├── style.css
│   └── app.js
└── templates/
    └── index.html
```

## ⚙️ Setup & Installation

**1. Clone the repository**
```bash
git clone https://github.com/rbbhadiyar/QuizBuddy.git
cd QuizBuddy
```

**2. Install dependencies**
```bash
pip install -r requirements.txt
```

**3. Configure your API key**

Create a `.env` file in the root directory:
```
OPENAI_API_KEY=your_groq_api_key_here
```
Get your free Groq API key at: https://console.groq.com

**4. Run the app**
```bash
python app.py
```

Open **http://localhost:5000** in your browser.

## ✨ Features

- 📄 Upload **PDF** or **DOCX** files
- 🔗 Extract content from any **URL**
- 🤖 Auto-detects **key topics** using AI
- 📝 Generates **MCQs** with 4 options, correct answer & explanation
- 🃏 Generates **Flashcards** with flip animation
- 🎯 Three **difficulty levels** — Easy, Medium, Hard
- 🔍 **Topic filter** to focus on specific subjects
- 📊 **Score tracking** after MCQ submission
- ⬇️ **Export quiz** as JSON

## 🖥️ Screenshot

### Input & Configuration
![Input Screen](assets/Screenshot%202026-05-20%20145637.png)

## 🎥 Demo

https://github.com/user-attachments/assets/0beb6749-f866-49b7-99b9-2f8a9db5dc4c
```

}

});

import docx
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup


def extract_from_pdf(file) -> str:
    doc = fitz.open(stream=file.read(), filetype="pdf")
    return "\n".join(page.get_text() for page in doc)


def extract_from_docx(file) -> str:
    document = docx.Document(file)
    return "\n".join(p.text for p in document.paragraphs if p.text.strip())


def extract_from_url(url: str) -> str:
    """Basic extraction — caller can replace clean_text logic later."""
    response = requests.get(url, timeout=10, headers={"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"})
    response.raise_for_status()
    soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, "html.parser")

    # Remove noise tags
    for tag in soup(["script", "style", "nav", "footer", "header", "aside"]):
        tag.decompose()

    # TODO: plug in your custom cleaning code here
    raw_text = soup.get_text(separator="\n")
    lines = [line.strip() for line in raw_text.splitlines() if line.strip()]
    return "\n".join(lines)

### File: app.py
```
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify, render_template
from flask_cors import CORS
from extractors import extract_from_pdf, extract_from_docx, extract_from_url
from quiz_generator import generate_quiz

app = Flask(__name__)
CORS(app)

ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS = {"pdf", "docx"}


def allowed_file(filename: str) -> bool:
    return "." in filename and filename.rsplit(".", 1)[1].lower() in ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS


@app.route("/")
def index():
    return render_template("index.html")


@app.route("/api/extract", methods=["POST"])
def extract():
    """Extract text from uploaded file or URL."""
    text = ""

    if "file" in request.files:
        file = request.files["file"]
        if not allowed_file(file.filename):
            return jsonify({"error": "Only PDF and DOCX files are supported."}), 400
        ext = file.filename.rsplit(".", 1)[1].lower()
        text = extract_from_pdf(file) if ext == "pdf" else extract_from_docx(file)

    elif request.json and request.json.get("url"):
        try:
            text = extract_from_url(request.json["url"])
        except Exception as e:
            return jsonify({"error": f"URL extraction failed: {str(e)}"}), 400
    else:
        return jsonify({"error": "Provide a file or URL."}), 400

    if not text.strip():
        return jsonify({"error": "No text could be extracted."}), 400

    return jsonify({"text": text[:8000], "char_count": len(text)})


@app.route("/api/generate", methods=["POST"])
def generate():
    """Generate quiz from extracted text."""
    data = request.json
    required = ["text", "mode", "difficulty"]
    if not all(k in data for k in required):
        return jsonify({"error": f"Missing fields: {required}"}), 400

    try:
        result = generate_quiz(
            text=data["text"],
            mode=data["mode"],           # mcq | flashcard | both
            difficulty=data["difficulty"],  # easy | medium | hard
            topic_filter=data.get("topic_filter", ""),
            count=int(data.get("count", 5)),
        )
        return jsonify(result)
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({"error": str(e)}), 500


if __name__ == "__main__":
    app.run(debug=True)
```

### File: extractors.py
```
import fitz  # PyMuPDF
import docx
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup


def extract_from_pdf(file) -> str:
    doc = fitz.open(stream=file.read(), filetype="pdf")
    return "\n".join(page.get_text() for page in doc)


def extract_from_docx(file) -> str:
    document = docx.Document(file)
    return "\n".join(p.text for p in document.paragraphs if p.text.strip())


def extract_from_url(url: str) -> str:
    """Basic extraction — caller can replace clean_text logic later."""
    response = requests.get(url, timeout=10, headers={"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"})
    response.raise_for_status()
    soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, "html.parser")

    # Remove noise tags
    for tag in soup(["script", "style", "nav", "footer", "header", "aside"]):
        tag.decompose()

    # TODO: plug in your custom cleaning code here
    raw_text = soup.get_text(separator="\n")
    lines = [line.strip() for line in raw_text.splitlines() if line.strip()]
    return "\n".join(lines)
```

### File: quiz_generator.py
```
import json
import os
from openai import OpenAI
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()
client = OpenAI(
    api_key=os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY"),
    base_url="https://api.groq.com/openai/v1"
)

DIFFICULTY_HINTS = {
    "easy": "Use simple language. Focus on basic definitions and facts.",
    "medium": "Include conceptual understanding and application-based questions.",
    "hard": "Include analysis, inference, and multi-step reasoning questions.",
}


def _chat(messages: list, model="llama-3.1-8b-instant") -> str:
    response = client.chat.completions.create(model=model, messages=messages)
    return response.choices[0].message.content.strip()


# ── Chain Step 1: Extract key topics from raw text ──────────────────────────
def extract_topics(text: str, topic_filter: str = None) -> str:
    prompt = f"Extract the main educational topics from the following text as a concise bullet list."
    if topic_filter:
        prompt += f" Focus only on topics related to: {topic_filter}."
    prompt += f"\n\nText:\n{text[:6000]}"

    return _chat([
        {"role": "system", "content": "You are an expert educator and content analyst."},
        {"role": "user", "content": prompt},
    ])


# ── Chain Step 2: Generate MCQs from topics + text ──────────────────────────
def generate_mcqs(text: str, topics: str, difficulty: str, count: int = 5) -> list:
    hint = DIFFICULTY_HINTS.get(difficulty, DIFFICULTY_HINTS["medium"])
    prompt = f"""You are a quiz generator. Based on the topics and source text below, generate {count} multiple-choice questions.

Difficulty: {difficulty.upper()} — {hint}

Topics:
{topics}

Source Text (excerpt):
{text[:5000]}

Return ONLY a JSON array in this exact format:
[
  {{
    "question": "...",
    "options": {{"A": "...", "B": "...", "C": "...", "D": "..."}},
    "answer": "A",
    "explanation": "..."
  }}
]"""

    raw = _chat([
        {"role": "system", "content": "You are a precise quiz generator. Output only valid JSON."},
        {"role": "user", "content": prompt},
    ])
    return _parse_json(raw)


# ── Chain Step 3: Generate Flashcards ───────────────────────────────────────
def generate_flashcards(text: str, topics: str, difficulty: str, count: int = 5) -> list:
    hint = DIFFICULTY_HINTS.get(difficulty, DIFFICULTY_HINTS["medium"])
    prompt = f"""Generate {count} flashcards from the topics and text below.

Difficulty: {difficulty.upper()} — {hint}

Topics:
{topics}

Source Text (excerpt):
{text[:5000]}

Return ONLY a JSON array:
[
  {{
    "front": "Question or term",
    "back": "Answer or definition"
  }}
]"""

    raw = _chat([
        {"role": "system", "content": "You are a flashcard creator. Output only valid JSON."},
        {"role": "user", "content": prompt},
    ])
    return _parse_json(raw)


# ── Output Parser ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    """Strip markdown fences and parse JSON safely."""
    cleaned = raw.strip()
    if cle

### File: README.md
```
# 🧠 QuizBuddy — AI Study Buddy

QuizBuddy is an AI-powered study assistant that transforms your study material into interactive quizzes and flashcards instantly. Simply upload a PDF, Word document, or paste a URL — QuizBuddy extracts the content, detects key topics using prompt chaining, and generates MCQs or flashcards tailored to your chosen difficulty level. It's built to make revision faster, smarter, and more engaging.

## 🛠 Tech Stack

| Layer | Technology |
|---|---|
| Backend | Python, Flask, Flask-CORS |
| AI / LLM | Groq API (`llama-3.1-8b-instant`) via OpenAI-compatible SDK |
| PDF Extraction | PyMuPDF (fitz) |
| DOCX Extraction | python-docx |
| URL Extraction | Requests + BeautifulSoup4 |
| Frontend | HTML, CSS, Vanilla JavaScript |
| Config | python-dotenv |

## 📁 Project Structure

```
QuizBuddy/
├── app.py              # Flask server & API routes
├── extractors.py       # PDF, DOCX, URL text extraction
├── quiz_generator.py   # Prompt chaining + output parsing
├── requirements.txt    # Python dependencies
├── .env                # API key (not pushed to GitHub)
├── assets/             # Screenshots & demo
├── static/
│   ├── style.css
│   └── app.js
└── templates/
    └── index.html
```

## ⚙️ Setup & Installation

**1. Clone the repository**
```bash
git clone https://github.com/rbbhadiyar/QuizBuddy.git
cd QuizBuddy
```

**2. Install dependencies**
```bash
pip install -r requirements.txt
```

**3. Configure your API key**

Create a `.env` file in the root directory:
```
OPENAI_API_KEY=your_groq_api_key_here
```
Get your free Groq API key at: https://console.groq.com

**4. Run the app**
```bash
python app.py
```

Open **http://localhost:5000** in your browser.

## ✨ Features

- 📄 Upload **PDF** or **DOCX** files
- 🔗 Extract content from any **URL**
- 🤖 Auto-detects **key topics** using AI
- 📝 Generates **MCQs** with 4 options, correct answer & explanation
- 🃏 Generates **Flashcards** with flip animation
- 🎯 Three **difficulty levels** — Easy, Medium, Hard
- 🔍 **Topic filter** to focus on specific subjects
- 📊 **Score tracking** after MCQ submission
- ⬇️ **Export quiz** as JSON

### File: app.py
```
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify, render_template
from flask_cors import CORS
from extractors import extract_from_pdf, extract_from_docx, extract_from_url
from quiz_generator import generate_quiz

app = Flask(__name__)
CORS(app)

ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS = {"pdf", "docx"}


def allowed_file(filename: str) -> bool:
    return "." in filename and filename.rsplit(".", 1)[1].lower() in ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS


@app.route("/")
def index():
    return render_template("index.html")


@app.route("/api/extract", methods=["POST"])
def extract():
    """Extract text from uploaded file or URL."""
    text = ""

    if "file" in request.files:
        file = request.files["file"]
        if not allowed_file(file.filename):
            return jsonify({"error": "Only PDF and DOCX files are supported."}), 400
        ext = file.filename.rsplit(".", 1)[1].lower()
        text = extract_from_pdf(file) if ext == "pdf" else extract_from_docx(file)

    elif request.json and request.json.get("url"):
        try:
            text = extract_from_url(request.json["url"])
        except Exception as e:
            return jsonify({"error": f"URL extraction failed: {str(e)}"}), 400
    else:
        return jsonify({"error": "Provide a file or URL."}), 400

    if not text.strip():
        return jsonify({"error": "No text could be extracted."}), 400

    return jsonify({"text": text[:8000], "char_count": len(text)})


@app.route("/api/generate", methods=["POST"])
def generate():
    """Generate quiz from extracted text."""
    data = request.json
    required = ["text", "mode", "difficulty"]
    if not all(k in data for k in required):
        return jsonify({"error": f"Missing fields: {required}"}), 400

    try:
        result = generate_quiz(
            text=data["text"],
            mode=data["mode"],           # mcq | flashcard | both
            difficulty=data["difficulty"],  # easy | medium | hard
            topic_filter=data.get("topic_filter", ""),
            count=int(data.get("count", 5)),
        )
        return jsonify(result)
    except Exception as e:
        return jsonify({"error": str(e)}), 500


if __name__ == "__main__":
    app.run(debug=True)
```

### File: extractors.py
```
import fitz  # PyMuPDF
import docx
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup


def extract_from_pdf(file) -> str:
    doc = fitz.open(stream=file.read(), filetype="pdf")
    return "\n".join(page.get_text() for page in doc)


def extract_from_docx(file) -> str:
    document = docx.Document(file)
    return "\n".join(p.text for p in document.paragraphs if p.text.strip())


def extract_from_url(url: str) -> str:
    """Basic extraction — caller can replace clean_text logic later."""
    response = requests.get(url, timeout=10, headers={"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"})
    response.raise_for_status()
    soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, "html.parser")

    # Remove noise tags
    for tag in soup(["script", "style", "nav", "footer", "header", "aside"]):
        tag.decompose()

    # TODO: plug in your custom cleaning code here
    raw_text = soup.get_text(separator="\n")
    lines = [line.strip() for line in raw_text.splitlines() if line.strip()]
    return "\n".join(lines)
```

### File: quiz_generator.py
```
import json
import os
from openai import OpenAI
from dotenv import load_dotenv

load_dotenv()
client = OpenAI(
    api_key=os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY"),
    base_url="https://api.groq.com/openai/v1"
)

DIFFICULTY_HINTS = {
    "easy": "Use simple language. Focus on basic definitions and facts.",
    "medium": "Include conceptual understanding and application-based questions.",
    "hard": "Include analysis, inference, and multi-step reasoning questions.",
}


def _chat(messages: list, model="llama-3.1-8b-instant") -> str:
    response = client.chat.completions.create(model=model, messages=messages)
    return response.choices[0].message.content.strip()


# ── Chain Step 1: Extract key topics from raw text ──────────────────────────
def extract_topics(text: str, topic_filter: str = None) -> str:
    prompt = f"Extract the main educational topics from the following text as a concise bullet list."
    if topic_filter:
        prompt += f" Focus only on topics related to: {topic_filter}."
    prompt += f"\n\nText:\n{text[:6000]}"

    return _chat([
        {"role": "system", "content": "You are an expert educator and content analyst."},
        {"role": "user", "content": prompt},
    ])


# ── Chain Step 2: Generate MCQs from topics + text ──────────────────────────
def generate_mcqs(text: str, topics: str, difficulty: str, count: int = 5) -> list:
    hint = DIFFICULTY_HINTS.get(difficulty, DIFFICULTY_HINTS["medium"])
    prompt = f"""You are a quiz generator. Based on the topics and source text below, generate {count} multiple-choice questions.

Difficulty: {difficulty.upper()} — {hint}

Topics:
{topics}

Source Text (excerpt):
{text[:5000]}

Return ONLY a JSON array in this exact format:
[
  {{
    "question": "...",
    "options": {{"A": "...", "B": "...", "C": "...", "D": "..."}},
    "answer": "A",
    "explanation": "..."
  }}
]"""

    raw = _chat([
        {"role": "system", "content": "You are a precise quiz generator. Output only valid JSON."},
        {"role": "user", "content": prompt},
    ])
    return _parse_json(raw)


# ── Chain Step 3: Generate Flashcards ───────────────────────────────────────
def generate_flashcards(text: str, topics: str, difficulty: str, count: int = 5) -> list:
    hint = DIFFICULTY_HINTS.get(difficulty, DIFFICULTY_HINTS["medium"])
    prompt = f"""Generate {count} flashcards from the topics and text below.

Difficulty: {difficulty.upper()} — {hint}

Topics:
{topics}

Source Text (excerpt):
{text[:5000]}

Return ONLY a JSON array:
[
  {{
    "front": "Question or term",
    "back": "Answer or definition"
  }}
]"""

    raw = _chat([
        {"role": "system", "content": "You are a flashcard creator. Output only valid JSON."},
        {"role": "user", "content": prompt},
    ])
    return _parse_json(raw)


# ── Output Parser ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
def _parse_json(raw: str) -> list:
    """Strip markdown fences and parse JSON safely."""
    cleaned = raw.strip()
    if cle

### File: README.md
```
# 🧠 QuizBuddy — AI Study Buddy

QuizBuddy is an AI-powered study assistant that transforms your study material into interactive quizzes and flashcards instantly. Simply upload a PDF, Word document, or paste a URL — QuizBuddy extracts the content, detects key topics using prompt chaining, and generates MCQs or flashcards tailored to your chosen difficulty level. It's built to make revision faster, smarter, and more engaging.

## 🛠 Tech Stack

| Layer | Technology |
|---|---|
| Backend | Python, Flask, Flask-CORS |
| AI / LLM | Groq API (`llama-3.1-8b-instant`) via OpenAI-compatible SDK |
| PDF Extraction | PyMuPDF (fitz) |
| DOCX Extraction | python-docx |
| URL Extraction | Requests + BeautifulSoup4 |
| Frontend | HTML, CSS, Vanilla JavaScript |
| Config | python-dotenv |

## 📁 Project Structure

```
QuizBuddy/
├── app.py              # Flask server & API routes
├── extractors.py       # PDF, DOCX, URL text extraction
├── quiz_generator.py   # Prompt chaining + output parsing
├── requirements.txt    # Python dependencies
├── .env                # API key (not pushed to GitHub)
├── assets/             # Screenshots & demo
├── static/
│   ├── style.css
│   └── app.js
└── templates/
    └── index.html
```

## ⚙️ Setup & Installation

**1. Clone the repository**
```bash
git clone https://github.com/rbbhadiyar/QuizBuddy.git
cd QuizBuddy
```

**2. Install dependencies**
```bash
pip install -r requirements.txt
```

**3. Configure your API key**

Create a `.env` file in the root directory:
```
OPENAI_API_KEY=your_groq_api_key_here
```
Get your free Groq API key at: https://console.groq.com

**4. Run the app**
```bash
python app.py
```

Open **http://localhost:5000** in your browser.

## ✨ Features

- 📄 Upload **PDF** or **DOCX** files
- 🔗 Extract content from any **URL**
- 🤖 Auto-detects **key topics** using AI
- 📝 Generates **MCQs** with 4 options, correct answer & explanation
- 🃏 Generates **Flashcards** with flip animation
- 🎯 Three **difficulty levels** — Easy, Medium, Hard
- 🔍 **Topic filter** to focus on specific subjects
- 📊 **Score tracking** after MCQ submission
- ⬇️ **Export quiz** as JSON

@test_app.route("/check_plagiarism", methods=["POST"])
def check_plagiarism():
    """API Endpoint to receive files and return plagiarism results."""
    uploaded_files = request.files.getlist("files")

    # Store file contents for highlighting
    file_contents = {}
    for file in uploaded_files:
        file_contents[file.filename] = file.read().decode("utf-8")
        file.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer for processing

    plagiarism_results, common_matches = process_files(uploaded_files)

    # Format results for the frontend
    formatted_results = {}
    file_names = [file.filename for file in uploaded_files]

    for i in range(len(file_names)):
        formatted_results[file_names[i]] = []
        for j in range(len(file_names)):
            if i != j:
                key = f"{i}_{j}"
                if key in plagiarism_results:
                    formatted_results[file_names[i]].append(
                        {
                            "file": file_names[j],
                            "plagiarism": plagiarism_results[key],
                            "matches": common_matches[key],
                        }
                    )
                else:
                    formatted_results[file_names[i]].append(
                        {"file": file_names[j], "plagiarism": 0, "matches": None}
                    )

    return jsonify(
        {
            "results": formatted_results,
            "file_names": file_names,
            "file_contents": file_contents,
        }
    )
@test_app.route('/check_text_similarity', methods=['POST'])
def check_text_similarity():
    uploaded_files = request.files.getlist('files')
    
    if len(uploaded_files) < 2:
        return jsonify({"error": "Please upload at least two text files."}), 400

    # Store file contents (convert to text first)
    file_contents = {}
    valid_files = []
    
    for file in uploaded_files:
        # Convert file to text content
        content = convert_file_to_txt(file)
        
        if content.strip():  # Only process if we got some content
            file_contents[file.filename] = content
            valid_files.append(file)
        else:
            print(f"Warning: No content extracted from {file.filename}")
        
        file.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer

    if len(valid_files) < 2:
        return jsonify({"error": "At least two files must contain readable content."}), 400

    result = process_tfidf_files(valid_files)
    if result is None:

### File: utils\file_converter.py
```
import os
import tempfile
from PyPDF2 import PdfReader
from docx import Document

def convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a PDF FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        reader = PdfReader(file_storage.stream)
        text_content = ""
        for page in reader.pages:
            text_content += page.extract_text() + "\n"
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting PDF '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a DOCX FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=False, suffix='.docx') as temp_file:
            file_storage.save(temp_file.name)
            
        document = Document(temp_file.name)
        text_content = ""
        for paragraph in document.paragraphs:
            text_content += paragraph.text + "\n"
        
        os.unlink(temp_file.name)
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting DOCX '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_file_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a file to text based on its extension.
    """
    filename = file_storage.filename.lower()
    
    if filename.endswith('.pdf'):
        return convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.docx') or filename.endswith('.doc'):
        return convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.txt'):
        try:
            content = file_storage.read().decode('utf-8')
            file_storage.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer
            return content
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading TXT file '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
            return ""
    else:
        print(f"Unsupported file type: {filename}")
        return ""
```

### File: utils\test_findMatch.py
```
import hashlib
import re
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from utils.file_converter import convert_file_to_txt


def preprocess_text(text):
    """Preprocess text by removing punctuation and converting to lowercase."""
    text = re.sub(r"[^\w\s]", "", text).lower()
    return text


def generate_kgrams(text, k):
    """Generate k-grams from the text with their positions."""
    kgrams = []
    for i in range(len(text) - k + 1):
        kgrams.append({"text": text[i : i + k], "start": i, "end": i + k})
    return kgrams


def hash_kgrams(kgrams):
    """Hash each k-gram using SHA-256 and keep position info."""
    hashed_kgrams = []
    for kgram in kgrams:
        hash_object = hashlib.sha256(kgram["text"].encode())
        hashed_kgrams.append(
            {
                "hash": int(hash_object.hexdigest(), 16),
                "start": kgram["start"],
                "end": kgram["end"],
            }
        )
    return hashed_kgrams


def winnow(hashed_kgrams, w):
    """Winnowing algorithm to select fingerprints with positions."""
    if not hashed_kgrams or w <= 0:
        return []

    fingerprints = []
    window = [float("inf")] * w
    r = 0
    min_index = 0

    for i, hashed_kgram in enumerate(hashed_kgrams):
        r = i % w
        window[r] = hashed_kgram["hash"]

        if min_index == r:
            # Scan leftward to find new minimum
            min_index = r
            for j in range(r - 1, -1, -1):
                if window[j] < window[min_index]:
                    min_index = j
            for j in range(w - 1, r, -1):
                if window[j] < window[min_index]:
                    min_index = j

            # Ensure we don't go out of bounds
            selected_index = max(0, min(i - (r - min_index), len(hashed_kgrams) - 1))
            fingerprints.append(
                {
                    "hash": window[min_index],
                    "start": hashed_kgrams[selected_index]["start"],
                    "end": hashed_kgrams[selected_index]["end"],
                }
            )
        else:
            # Compare with current minimum and update if necessary
            if window[r] <= window[min_index]:
                min_index = r
                fingerprints.append(
                    {
                        "hash": window[r],
                        "start": hashed_kgram["start"],
                        "end": hashed_kgram["end"],
                    }
                )

    return fingerprints


def compare_fingerprints(fingerprints_list, original_texts):
    """Compare fingerprints across documents and return matches with positions."""
    plagiarism_results = {}
    common_matches = {}

    for i, fingerprints_i in enumerate(fingerprints_list):
        for j, fingerprints_j in enumerate(fingerprints_list):
            if i != j:
                # Convert to sets of hashes for quick lookup
                set_

import os
import tempfile
from PyPDF2 import PdfReader
from docx import Document

def convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a PDF FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        reader = PdfReader(file_storage.stream)
        text_content = ""
        for page in reader.pages:
            text_content += page.extract_text() + "\n"
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting PDF '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a DOCX FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=False, suffix='.docx') as temp_file:
            file_storage.save(temp_file.name)
            
        document = Document(temp_file.name)
        text_content = ""
        for paragraph in document.paragraphs:
            text_content += paragraph.text + "\n"
        
        os.unlink(temp_file.name)
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting DOCX '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_file_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a file to text based on its extension.
    """
    filename = file_storage.filename.lower()
    
    if filename.endswith('.pdf'):
        return convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.docx') or filename.endswith('.doc'):
        return convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.txt'):
        try:
            content = file_storage.read().decode('utf-8')
            file_storage.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer
            return content
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading TXT file '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
            return ""
    else:
        print(f"Unsupported file type: {filename}")
        return ""

* Compare text similarity across different file formats

* Modular architecture for easy maintenance and scalability

def check_plagiarism():
    """API Endpoint to receive files and return plagiarism results."""
    uploaded_files = request.files.getlist("files")

    # Store file contents for highlighting
    file_contents = {}
    for file in uploaded_files:
        file_contents[file.filename] = file.read().decode("utf-8")
        file.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer for processing

                        {
                            "file": file_names[j],
                            "plagiarism": plagiarism_results[key],
                            "matches": common_matches[key],
                        }
                    )
                else:
                    formatted_results[file_names[i]].append(
                        {"file": file_names[j], "plagiarism": 0, "matches": None}
                    )

    return jsonify(
        {
            "results": formatted_results,
            "file_names": file_names,
            "file_contents": file_contents,
        }

### File: utils\file_converter.py
```
import os
import tempfile
from PyPDF2 import PdfReader
from docx import Document

def convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a PDF FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        reader = PdfReader(file_storage.stream)
        text_content = ""
        for page in reader.pages:
            text_content += page.extract_text() + "\n"
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting PDF '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a DOCX FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=False, suffix='.docx') as temp_file:
            file_storage.save(temp_file.name)
            
        document = Document(temp_file.name)
        text_content = ""
        for paragraph in document.paragraphs:
            text_content += paragraph.text + "\n"
        
        os.unlink(temp_file.name)
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting DOCX '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_file_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a file to text based on its extension.
    """
    filename = file_storage.filename.lower()
    
    if filename.endswith('.pdf'):
        return convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.docx') or filename.endswith('.doc'):
        return convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.txt'):
        try:
            content = file_storage.read().decode('utf-8')
            file_storage.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer
            return content
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading TXT file '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
            return ""
    else:
        print(f"Unsupported file type: {filename}")
        return ""
```

### File: utils\test_findMatch.py
```
import hashlib
import re
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from utils.file_converter import convert_file_to_txt


def preprocess_text(text):
    """Preprocess text by removing punctuation and converting to lowercase."""
    text = re.sub(r"[^\w\s]", "", text).lower()
    return text


def generate_kgrams(text, k):
    """Generate k-grams from the text with their positions."""
    kgrams = []
    for i in range(len(text) - k + 1):
        kgrams.append({"text": text[i : i + k], "start": i, "end": i + k})
    return kgrams


def hash_kgrams(kgrams):
    """Hash each k-gram using SHA-256 and keep position info."""
    hashed_kgrams = []
    for kgram in kgrams:
        hash_object = hashlib.sha256(kgram["text"].encode())
        hashed_kgrams.append(
            {
                "hash": int(hash_object.hexdigest(), 16),
                "start": kgram["start"],
                "end": kgram["end"],
            }
        )
    return hashed_kgrams


def winnow(hashed_kgrams, w):
    """Winnowing algorithm to select fingerprints with positions."""
    if not hashed_kgrams or w <= 0:
        return []

    fingerprints = []
    window = [float("inf")] * w
    r = 0
    min_index = 0

    for i, hashed_kgram in enumerate(hashed_kgrams):
        r = i % w
        window[r] = hashed_kgram["hash"]

        if min_index == r:
            # Scan leftward to find new minimum
            min_index = r
            for j in range(r - 1, -1, -1):
                if window[j] < window[min_index]:
                    min_index = j
            for j in range(w - 1, r, -1):
                if window[j] < window[min_index]:
                    min_index = j

            # Ensure we don't go out of bounds
            selected_index = max(0, min(i - (r - min_index), len(hashed_kgrams) - 1))
            fingerprints.append(
                {
                    "hash": window[min_index],
                    "start": hashed_kgrams[selected_index]["start"],
                    "end": hashed_kgrams[selected_index]["end"],
                }
            )
        else:
            # Compare with current minimum and update if necessary
            if window[r] <= window[min_index]:
                min_index = r
                fingerprints.append(
                    {
                        "hash": window[r],
                        "start": hashed_kgram["start"],
                        "end": hashed_kgram["end"],
                    }
                )

    return fingerprints


def compare_fingerprints(fingerprints_list, original_texts):
    """Compare fingerprints across documents and return matches with positions."""
    plagiarism_results = {}
    common_matches = {}

    for i, fingerprints_i in enumerate(fingerprints_list):
        for j, fingerprints_j in enumerate(fingerprints_list):
            if i != j:
                # Convert to sets of hashes for quick lookup
                set_

import os
import tempfile
from PyPDF2 import PdfReader
from docx import Document

def convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a PDF FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        reader = PdfReader(file_storage.stream)
        text_content = ""
        for page in reader.pages:
            text_content += page.extract_text() + "\n"
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting PDF '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a DOCX FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=False, suffix='.docx') as temp_file:
            file_storage.save(temp_file.name)
            
        document = Document(temp_file.name)
        text_content = ""
        for paragraph in document.paragraphs:
            text_content += paragraph.text + "\n"
        
        os.unlink(temp_file.name)
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting DOCX '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_file_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a file to text based on its extension.
    """
    filename = file_storage.filename.lower()
    
    if filename.endswith('.pdf'):
        return convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.docx') or filename.endswith('.doc'):
        return convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.txt'):
        try:
            content = file_storage.read().decode('utf-8')
            file_storage.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer
            return content
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading TXT file '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
            return ""
    else:
        print(f"Unsupported file type: {filename}")
        return ""

# Plagiarism Detection and Text Similarity Checker
==============================================

## Description
This project is a Python-based application designed for plagiarism detection and text similarity checking between multiple files. It utilizes a file converter to handle different file formats (PDF, DOCX, TXT) and processes them to detect plagiarism and check for text similarity.

## Features
*   Handles different file formats (PDF, DOCX, TXT)
*   Provides API endpoints for receiving files and returning results
*   Utilizes a modular design for easy addition of new file formats and processing algorithms
*   Includes functions for preprocessing text, generating fingerprints, and comparing them for plagiarism detection

## Installation Steps
1.  Clone the repository using `git clone`
2.  Install the required dependencies using `pip install -r requirements.txt`
3.  Run the application using `python test_app.py`

## Usage
1.  Send a request to the API endpoint with files attached
2.  The application will convert the files to text format, preprocess the text, generate fingerprints, and compare them for plagiarism detection and text similarity
3.  The results will be returned through the API endpoint

## Contributing
Contributions are welcome and encouraged. To contribute, please fork the repository, make changes, and submit a pull request.

## 🧠 How It Works
The system works end-to-end as follows:
1.  **File Conversion**: The `utils/file_converter.py` module converts different file formats (PDF, DOCX, TXT) to text format. This is essential for the application to process files regardless of their original format.
2.  **Text Preprocessing**: The `utils/test_findMatch.py` module preprocesses the text by removing punctuation and converting to lowercase. This step prepares the text for fingerprint generation.
3.  **Fingerprint Generation**: The `utils/test_findMatch.py` module generates fingerprints from the preprocessed text using k-grams and hashing. These fingerprints are used for plagiarism detection and text similarity checking.
4.  **Fingerprint Comparison**: The `utils/test_findMatch.py` module compares the fingerprints across documents to detect plagiarism and text similarity.
5.  **API Endpoints**: The `test_app.py` module provides API endpoints for receiving files and returning results. It integrates the `utils` modules and ensures seamless communication between the client and server.

## 🚀 Quick Start Guide
### Step 1: Clone the Repository
```bash
git clone https://github.com/your-username/plagiarism-detection.git
```
### Step 2: Install Dependencies
```bash
pip install -r requirements.txt
```
### Step 3: Run the Application
```bash
python test_app.py
```
### Step 4: Send a Request to the API Endpoint
Use a tool like `curl` or a REST client to send a request to the API endpoint with files attached. For example:
```bash

```

from flask import Flask, request, jsonify, render_template
from utils.test_findMatch import process_files

from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity

def index():
    """Render the main HTML page."""
    return render_template("test_index.html")


@test_app.route("/check_plagiarism", methods=["POST"])
def check_plagiarism():
    """API Endpoint to receive files and return plagiarism results."""
    uploaded_files = request.files.getlist("files")

    # Store file contents for highlighting
    file_contents = {}
    for file in uploaded_files:
        file_contents[file.filename] = file.read().decode("utf-8")
        file.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer for processing

    plagiarism_results, common_matches = process_files(uploaded_files)

    # Format results for the frontend
    formatted_results = {}
    file_names = [file.filename for file in uploaded_files]

    for i in range(len(file_names)):
        formatted_results[file_names[i]] = []
        for j in range(len(file_names)):
            if i != j:
                key = f"{i}_{j}"
                if key in plagiarism_results:
                    formatted_results[file_names[i]].append(
                        {
                            "file": file_names[j],
                            "plagiarism": plagiarism_results[key],
                            "matches": common_matches[key],
                        }
                    )
                else:
                    formatted_results[file_names[i]].append(
                        {"file": file_names[j], "plagiarism": 0, "matches": None}
                    )

    return jsonify(
        {
            "results": formatted_results,
            "file_names": file_names,
            "file_contents": file_contents,
        }
    )
@test_app.route('/check_text_similarity', methods=['POST'])
def check_text_similarity():
    uploaded_files = request.files.getlist('files')
    
    if len(uploaded_files) < 2:
        return jsonify({"error": "Please upload at least two text files."}), 400

    # Store file contents (convert to text first)
    file_contents = {}
    valid_files = []
    
    for file in uploaded_files:
        # Convert file to text content
        content = convert_file_to_txt(file)
        
        if content.strip():  # Only process if we got some content
            file_contents[file.filename] = content
            valid_files.append(file)
        else:
            print(f"Warning: No content extracted from {file.filename}")
        
        file.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer

    if len(valid_files) < 2:
        return jsonify({"error": "At least two files must contain readable content."}), 400

### File: utils\file_converter.py
```
import os
import tempfile
from PyPDF2 import PdfReader
from docx import Document

def convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a PDF FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        reader = PdfReader(file_storage.stream)
        text_content = ""
        for page in reader.pages:
            text_content += page.extract_text() + "\n"
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting PDF '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a DOCX FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=False, suffix='.docx') as temp_file:
            file_storage.save(temp_file.name)
            
        document = Document(temp_file.name)
        text_content = ""
        for paragraph in document.paragraphs:
            text_content += paragraph.text + "\n"
        
        os.unlink(temp_file.name)
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting DOCX '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_file_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a file to text based on its extension.
    """
    filename = file_storage.filename.lower()
    
    if filename.endswith('.pdf'):
        return convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.docx') or filename.endswith('.doc'):
        return convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.txt'):
        try:
            content = file_storage.read().decode('utf-8')
            file_storage.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer
            return content
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading TXT file '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
            return ""
    else:
        print(f"Unsupported file type: {filename}")
        return ""
```

### File: utils\test_findMatch.py
```
import hashlib
import re
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from utils.file_converter import convert_file_to_txt


def preprocess_text(text):
    """Preprocess text by removing punctuation and converting to lowercase."""
    text = re.sub(r"[^\w\s]", "", text).lower()
    return text


def generate_kgrams(text, k):
    """Generate k-grams from the text with their positions."""
    kgrams = []
    for i in range(len(text) - k + 1):
        kgrams.append({"text": text[i : i + k], "start": i, "end": i + k})
    return kgrams


def hash_kgrams(kgrams):
    """Hash each k-gram using SHA-256 and keep position info."""
    hashed_kgrams = []
    for kgram in kgrams:
        hash_object = hashlib.sha256(kgram["text"].encode())
        hashed_kgrams.append(
            {
                "hash": int(hash_object.hexdigest(), 16),
                "start": kgram["start"],
                "end": kgram["end"],
            }
        )
    return hashed_kgrams


def winnow(hashed_kgrams, w):
    """Winnowing algorithm to select fingerprints with positions."""
    if not hashed_kgrams or w <= 0:
        return []

    fingerprints = []
    window = [float("inf")] * w
    r = 0
    min_index = 0

    for i, hashed_kgram in enumerate(hashed_kgrams):
        r = i % w
        window[r] = hashed_kgram["hash"]

        if min_index == r:
            # Scan leftward to find new minimum
            min_index = r
            for j in range(r - 1, -1, -1):
                if window[j] < window[min_index]:
                    min_index = j
            for j in range(w - 1, r, -1):
                if window[j] < window[min_index]:
                    min_index = j

            # Ensure we don't go out of bounds
            selected_index = max(0, min(i - (r - min_index), len(hashed_kgrams) - 1))
            fingerprints.append(
                {
                    "hash": window[min_index],
                    "start": hashed_kgrams[selected_index]["start"],
                    "end": hashed_kgrams[selected_index]["end"],
                }
            )
        else:
            # Compare with current minimum and update if necessary
            if window[r] <= window[min_index]:
                min_index = r
                fingerprints.append(
                    {
                        "hash": window[r],
                        "start": hashed_kgram["start"],
                        "end": hashed_kgram["end"],
                    }
                )

    return fingerprints


def compare_fingerprints(fingerprints_list, original_texts):
    """Compare fingerprints across documents and return matches with positions."""
    plagiarism_results = {}
    common_matches = {}

    for i, fingerprints_i in enumerate(fingerprints_list):
        for j, fingerprints_j in enumerate(fingerprints_list):
            if i != j:
                # Convert to sets of hashes for quick lookup
                set_

    """

        for page in reader.pages:
            text_content += page.extract_text() + "\n"

        return ""

        print(f"Error converting DOCX '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")

    Converts a file to text based on its extension.

# Plagiarism Detector
A Python-based web application that provides a web interface for users to upload files and receive plagiarism and text similarity results.

## Description
The application utilizes a file converter utility to process files in various formats (PDF, DOCX, TXT) and calculate the similarity between them. The project's primary functionality involves converting files to plain text, preprocessing the text, generating k-grams, hashing k-grams, and comparing fingerprints across documents to detect plagiarism and calculate text similarity.

## Features
* Converts files from various formats (PDF, DOCX, TXT) to plain text
* Preprocesses text by removing punctuation and converting to lowercase
* Generates k-grams from the text with their positions
* Hashes each k-gram using SHA-256 and keeps position info
* Applies the winnowing algorithm to select fingerprints with positions
* Compares fingerprints across documents and returns matches with positions

## Installation Steps
1. Clone the repository using `git clone https://github.com/your-username/plagiarism-detector.git`
2. Install the required dependencies using `pip install -r requirements.txt`
3. Run the application using `python test_app.py`

## Usage
1. Upload files to the web application
2. The application will convert the files to plain text and calculate the similarity between them
3. The application will return the plagiarism and text similarity results

## Contributing
Contributions are welcome! To contribute, please fork the repository and submit a pull request with your changes.

## Dependencies
* Flask
* PyPDF2
* python-docx
* hashlib
* re
* utils.file_converter
* utils.test_findMatch

## 🧠 How It Works
The plagiarism detector application works as follows:
1. **File Upload**: Users upload files to the web application.
2. **File Conversion**: The `file_converter` module converts the uploaded files to plain text. This involves using libraries such as PyPDF2 and python-docx to read and write PDF and DOCX files, respectively.
3. **Text Preprocessing**: The `test_findMatch` module preprocesses the text by removing punctuation and converting to lowercase. This step is necessary to normalize the text and prepare it for further processing.
4. **K-gram Generation**: The `test_findMatch` module generates k-grams from the preprocessed text. K-grams are sequences of k items (in this case, characters) that are used to represent the text.
5. **K-gram Hashing**: The `test_findMatch` module hashes each k-gram using SHA-256 and keeps position info. This step is necessary to create a unique identifier for each k-gram.
6. **Winnowing**: The `test_findMatch` module applies the winnowing algorithm to select fingerprints with positions. Winnowing is a technique used to reduce the number of k-grams that need to be compared.
7. **Fingerprint Comparison**: The `test_findMatch` module compares fingerprints across documents and returns matches with positions. This step is necessary to detect plagiarism and calculate text similarity.
8. **Result Return**: The application returns the plagiarism and text similarity results to the user.

The application uses a modular design, with each module having a specific role in the overall functionality of the project. The `file_converter` module is responsible for converting files to plain text, while the `test_findMatch` module is responsible for preprocessing text, generating k-grams, hashing k-grams, and comparing fingerprints across documents. The application relies on several libraries and modules, including Flask, PyPDF2, python-docx, hashlib, and re."

```
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify, render_template
from utils.test_findMatch import process_files

from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from utils.test_findMatch import process_files, process_tfidf_files
from utils.file_converter import convert_file_to_txt

test_app = Flask(__name__)


@test_app.route("/")
def index():
    """Render the main HTML page."""
    return render_template("test_index.html")


@test_app.route("/check_plagiarism", methods=["POST"])
def check_plagiarism():
    """API Endpoint to receive files and return plagiarism results."""
    uploaded_files = request.files.getlist("files")

    # Store file contents for highlighting
    file_contents = {}
    for file in uploaded_files:
        file_contents[file.filename] = file.read().decode("utf-8")
        file.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer for processing

    plagiarism_results, common_matches = process_files(uploaded_files)

    # Format results for the frontend
    formatted_results = {}
    file_names = [file.filename for file in uploaded_files]

    for i in range(len(file_names)):
        formatted_results[file_names[i]] = []
        for j in range(len(file_names)):
            if i != j:
                key = f"{i}_{j}"
                if key in plagiarism_results:
                    formatted_results[file_names[i]].append(
                        {
                            "file": file_names[j],
                            "plagiarism": plagiarism_results[key],
                            "matches": common_matches[key],
                        }
                    )
                else:
                    formatted_results[file_names[i]].append(
                        {"file": file_names[j], "plagiarism": 0, "matches": None}
                    )

    return jsonify(
        {
            "results": formatted_results,
            "file_names": file_names,
            "file_contents": file_contents,
        }
    )
@test_app.route('/check_text_similarity', methods=['POST'])
def check_text_similarity():
    uploaded_files = request.files.getlist('files')
    
    if len(uploaded_files) < 2:
        return jsonify({"error": "Please upload at least two text files."}), 400

    # Store file contents (convert to text first)
    file_contents = {}
    valid_files = []
    
    for file in uploaded_files:
        # Convert file to text content
        content = convert_file_to_txt(file)
        
        if content.strip():  # Only process if we got some content
            file_contents[file.filename] = content
            valid_files.append(file)
        else:
            print(f"Warning: No content extracted from {file.filename}")
        
        file.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer

    if len(valid_files) < 2:
        return jsonify({"error": "At least two files must contain readable content."}), 400

    result = process_tfidf_files(valid_files)
    if result is None:
        return js

### File: utils\file_converter.py
```
import os
import tempfile
from PyPDF2 import PdfReader
from docx import Document

def convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a PDF FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        reader = PdfReader(file_storage.stream)
        text_content = ""
        for page in reader.pages:
            text_content += page.extract_text() + "\n"
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting PDF '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a DOCX FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=False, suffix='.docx') as temp_file:
            file_storage.save(temp_file.name)
            
        document = Document(temp_file.name)
        text_content = ""
        for paragraph in document.paragraphs:
            text_content += paragraph.text + "\n"
        
        os.unlink(temp_file.name)
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting DOCX '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_file_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a file to text based on its extension.
    """
    filename = file_storage.filename.lower()
    
    if filename.endswith('.pdf'):
        return convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.docx') or filename.endswith('.doc'):
        return convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.txt'):
        try:
            content = file_storage.read().decode('utf-8')
            file_storage.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer
            return content
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading TXT file '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
            return ""
    else:
        print(f"Unsupported file type: {filename}")
        return ""
```

### File: utils\test_findMatch.py
```
import hashlib
import re
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from utils.file_converter import convert_file_to_txt


def preprocess_text(text):
    """Preprocess text by removing punctuation and converting to lowercase."""
    text = re.sub(r"[^\w\s]", "", text).lower()
    return text


def generate_kgrams(text, k):
    """Generate k-grams from the text with their positions."""
    kgrams = []
    for i in range(len(text) - k + 1):
        kgrams.append({"text": text[i : i + k], "start": i, "end": i + k})
    return kgrams


def hash_kgrams(kgrams):
    """Hash each k-gram using SHA-256 and keep position info."""
    hashed_kgrams = []
    for kgram in kgrams:
        hash_object = hashlib.sha256(kgram["text"].encode())
        hashed_kgrams.append(
            {
                "hash": int(hash_object.hexdigest(), 16),
                "start": kgram["start"],
                "end": kgram["end"],
            }
        )
    return hashed_kgrams


def winnow(hashed_kgrams, w):
    """Winnowing algorithm to select fingerprints with positions."""
    if not hashed_kgrams or w <= 0:
        return []

    fingerprints = []
    window = [float("inf")] * w
    r = 0
    min_index = 0

    for i, hashed_kgram in enumerate(hashed_kgrams):
        r = i % w
        window[r] = hashed_kgram["hash"]

        if min_index == r:
            # Scan leftward to find new minimum
            min_index = r
            for j in range(r - 1, -1, -1):
                if window[j] < window[min_index]:
                    min_index = j
            for j in range(w - 1, r, -1):
                if window[j] < window[min_index]:
                    min_index = j

            # Ensure we don't go out of bounds
            selected_index = max(0, min(i - (r - min_index), len(hashed_kgrams) - 1))
            fingerprints.append(
                {
                    "hash": window[min_index],
                    "start": hashed_kgrams[selected_index]["start"],
                    "end": hashed_kgrams[selected_index]["end"],
                }
            )
        else:
            # Compare with current minimum and update if necessary
            if window[r] <= window[min_index]:
                min_index = r
                fingerprints.append(
                    {
                        "hash": window[r],
                        "start": hashed_kgram["start"],
                        "end": hashed_kgram["end"],
                    }
                )

    return fingerprints


def compare_fingerprints(fingerprints_list, original_texts):
    """Compare fingerprints across documents and return matches with positions."""
    plagiarism_results = {}
    common_matches = {}

    for i, fingerprints_i in enumerate(fingerprints_list):
        for j, fingerprints_j in enumerate(fingerprints_list):
            if i != j:
                # Convert to sets of hashes for quick lookup
                set_

# Project Title: Plagiarism Detection and Text Similarity Analysis Tool

## Description
This project is a Python-based application designed for plagiarism detection and text similarity analysis. It features a file converter that can handle various file types, such as PDF and DOCX, and converts them into text for further analysis. The application also includes a test interface built with Flask, allowing users to upload files and receive results on plagiarism and text similarity.

## Features
- File conversion: Supports conversion of PDF and DOCX files to text.
- Plagiarism detection: Analyzes uploaded files for plagiarism.
- Text similarity analysis: Compares text similarity between uploaded files.
- Test interface: Provides a web-based platform for users to interact with the application.

## Installation Steps
1. Clone the repository using `git clone`.
2. Install required dependencies using `pip install -r requirements.txt`.
3. Run the application using `python test_app.py`.

## Usage
1. Upload files through the test interface.
2. Select the analysis type (plagiarism detection or text similarity).
3. Receive results on plagiarism or text similarity.

## Contributing
Contributions are welcome. To contribute, please:
1. Fork the repository.
2. Make changes and commit them.
3. Create a pull request.

## 🧠 How It Works
The system works end-to-end as follows:

1. **File Upload**: The user uploads files through the test interface provided by `test_app.py`.
2. **File Conversion**: The uploaded files are converted into text using the functions in `file_converter.py`. This step is crucial for processing files in various formats.
3. **Text Preprocessing**: The converted text is preprocessed using functions in `test_findMatch.py`, such as `preprocess_text()`, to remove punctuation and convert to lowercase.
4. **K-gram Generation and Hashing**: The preprocessed text is then used to generate k-grams, which are hashed using SHA-256.
5. **Fingerprint Comparison**: The hashed k-grams are compared across documents using the `compare_fingerprints()` function to identify matches.
6. **Results Generation**: The results of the plagiarism detection or text similarity analysis are generated based on the comparison of fingerprints.
7. **Results Display**: The results are displayed to the user through the test interface provided by `test_app.py`.

The application's architecture is modular, with each component serving a distinct purpose. The `file_converter.py` module handles file conversion, while `test_findMatch.py` contains functions for text preprocessing, k-gram generation, hashing, and fingerprint comparison. The `test_app.py` file acts as the test interface, utilizing Flask to provide a web-based platform for user interaction. This modular approach allows for easy maintenance and extension of the application's functionality."

### File: test_app.py
```
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify, render_template
from utils.test_findMatch import process_files

from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from utils.test_findMatch import process_files, process_tfidf_files
from utils.file_converter import convert_file_to_txt

test_app = Flask(__name__)


@test_app.route("/")
def index():
    """Render the main HTML page."""
    return render_template("test_index.html")


@test_app.route("/check_plagiarism", methods=["POST"])
def check_plagiarism():
    """API Endpoint to receive files and return plagiarism results."""
    uploaded_files = request.files.getlist("files")

    # Store file contents for highlighting
    file_contents = {}
    for file in uploaded_files:
        file_contents[file.filename] = file.read().decode("utf-8")
        file.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer for processing

    plagiarism_results, common_matches = process_files(uploaded_files)

    # Format results for the frontend
    formatted_results = {}
    file_names = [file.filename for file in uploaded_files]

    for i in range(len(file_names)):
        formatted_results[file_names[i]] = []
        for j in range(len(file_names)):
            if i != j:
                key = f"{i}_{j}"
                if key in plagiarism_results:
                    formatted_results[file_names[i]].append(
                        {
                            "file": file_names[j],
                            "plagiarism": plagiarism_results[key],
                            "matches": common_matches[key],
                        }
                    )
                else:
                    formatted_results[file_names[i]].append(
                        {"file": file_names[j], "plagiarism": 0, "matches": None}
                    )

    return jsonify(
        {
            "results": formatted_results,
            "file_names": file_names,
            "file_contents": file_contents,
        }
    )
@test_app.route('/check_text_similarity', methods=['POST'])
def check_text_similarity():
    uploaded_files = request.files.getlist('files')
    
    if len(uploaded_files) < 2:
        return jsonify({"error": "Please upload at least two text files."}), 400

    # Store file contents (convert to text first)
    file_contents = {}
    valid_files = []
    
    for file in uploaded_files:
        # Convert file to text content
        content = convert_file_to_txt(file)
        
        if content.strip():  # Only process if we got some content
            file_contents[file.filename] = content
            valid_files.append(file)
        else:
            print(f"Warning: No content extracted from {file.filename}")
        
        file.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer

    if len(valid_files) < 2:
        return jsonify({"error": "At least two files must contain readable content."}), 400

    result = process_tfidf_files(valid_files)
    if result is None:
        return js

### File: utils\file_converter.py
```
import os
import tempfile
from PyPDF2 import PdfReader
from docx import Document

def convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a PDF FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        reader = PdfReader(file_storage.stream)
        text_content = ""
        for page in reader.pages:
            text_content += page.extract_text() + "\n"
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting PDF '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a DOCX FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=False, suffix='.docx') as temp_file:
            file_storage.save(temp_file.name)
            
        document = Document(temp_file.name)
        text_content = ""
        for paragraph in document.paragraphs:
            text_content += paragraph.text + "\n"
        
        os.unlink(temp_file.name)
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting DOCX '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_file_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a file to text based on its extension.
    """
    filename = file_storage.filename.lower()
    
    if filename.endswith('.pdf'):
        return convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.docx') or filename.endswith('.doc'):
        return convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.txt'):
        try:
            content = file_storage.read().decode('utf-8')
            file_storage.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer
            return content
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading TXT file '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
            return ""
    else:
        print(f"Unsupported file type: {filename}")
        return ""
```

### File: utils\test_findMatch.py
```
import hashlib
import re
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from utils.file_converter import convert_file_to_txt


def preprocess_text(text):
    """Preprocess text by removing punctuation and converting to lowercase."""
    text = re.sub(r"[^\w\s]", "", text).lower()
    return text


def generate_kgrams(text, k):
    """Generate k-grams from the text with their positions."""
    kgrams = []
    for i in range(len(text) - k + 1):
        kgrams.append({"text": text[i : i + k], "start": i, "end": i + k})
    return kgrams


def hash_kgrams(kgrams):
    """Hash each k-gram using SHA-256 and keep position info."""
    hashed_kgrams = []
    for kgram in kgrams:
        hash_object = hashlib.sha256(kgram["text"].encode())
        hashed_kgrams.append(
            {
                "hash": int(hash_object.hexdigest(), 16),
                "start": kgram["start"],
                "end": kgram["end"],
            }
        )
    return hashed_kgrams


def winnow(hashed_kgrams, w):
    """Winnowing algorithm to select fingerprints with positions."""
    if not hashed_kgrams or w <= 0:
        return []

    fingerprints = []
    window = [float("inf")] * w
    r = 0
    min_index = 0

    for i, hashed_kgram in enumerate(hashed_kgrams):
        r = i % w
        window[r] = hashed_kgram["hash"]

        if min_index == r:
            # Scan leftward to find new minimum
            min_index = r
            for j in range(r - 1, -1, -1):
                if window[j] < window[min_index]:
                    min_index = j
            for j in range(w - 1, r, -1):
                if window[j] < window[min_index]:
                    min_index = j

            # Ensure we don't go out of bounds
            selected_index = max(0, min(i - (r - min_index), len(hashed_kgrams) - 1))
            fingerprints.append(
                {
                    "hash": window[min_index],
                    "start": hashed_kgrams[selected_index]["start"],
                    "end": hashed_kgrams[selected_index]["end"],
                }
            )
        else:
            # Compare with current minimum and update if necessary
            if window[r] <= window[min_index]:
                min_index = r
                fingerprints.append(
                    {
                        "hash": window[r],
                        "start": hashed_kgram["start"],
                        "end": hashed_kgram["end"],
                    }
                )

    return fingerprints


def compare_fingerprints(fingerprints_list, original_texts):
    """Compare fingerprints across documents and return matches with positions."""
    plagiarism_results = {}
    common_matches = {}

    for i, fingerprints_i in enumerate(fingerprints_list):
        for j, fingerprints_j in enumerate(fingerprints_list):
            if i != j:
                # Convert to sets of hashes for quick lookup
                set_

The project is a Python-based application focused on utility and data processing tasks, specifically designed for plagiarism detection and text similarity analysis. It provides a web interface through a Flask application, allowing users to upload files and receive results on plagiarism and similarity between the uploaded documents. The project utilizes file conversion utilities to preprocess files into a comparable format and then applies algorithms for detecting plagiarism and measuring text similarity.

## 🧱 System Architecture Overview
The system architecture of the project is modular, with a clear separation of concerns between different components. The main application logic is handled by the `test_app.py` file, which serves as the entry point for the Flask web application. This file interacts with utility modules, such as `utils.file_converter.py` for file conversion and `utils.test_findMatch.py` for plagiarism detection and text similarity analysis. The application follows a microservices-like architecture, where each module is responsible for a specific task, enhancing maintainability and scalability.

## 📂 Folder-by-Folder Explanation
- **Root Directory**: Contains the main application file `test_app.py`, which is the central entry point for the Flask web application.
- **utils Folder**: This folder contains utility modules that provide specific functionalities.
  - `file_converter.py`: Provides functions for converting files from various formats (PDF, DOCX, TXT) into plain text.
  - `test_findMatch.py`: Offers functions for finding matches and detecting plagiarism between texts, utilizing techniques like text preprocessing, k-gram generation, hashing, and winnowing.

## ⚙️ Key Modules Breakdown
- **`test_app.py`**: This module is the main application file, responsible for handling HTTP requests, rendering the main HTML page, and providing API endpoints for checking plagiarism and text similarity.
- **`utils.file_converter.py`**: This module is crucial for file conversion, providing functions to convert PDF, DOCX, and TXT files into plain text for analysis.
