```", agent="Code Analyst", status="completed", output="### File: test_app.py
# Plagiarism Detection and Text Similarity Analysis Tool
==============================================

## Description
This project is a Python-based application designed for plagiarism detection and text similarity analysis. It provides a web interface through a Flask application, allowing users to upload files and receive results on plagiarism and similarity between the uploaded documents.

## Features
- **File Conversion**: Converts files from various formats (PDF, DOCX, TXT) into plain text for analysis.
- **Plagiarism Detection**: Utilizes algorithms such as text preprocessing, k-gram generation, hashing, and winnowing to detect plagiarism between documents.
- **Text Similarity Analysis**: Compares documents to find matches and measure text similarity.
- **Web Interface**: Provides a user-friendly interface for uploading files and viewing results.

## Installation Steps
1. Clone the repository: `git clone https://github.com/your-repo/plagiarism-detection.git`
2. Install required dependencies: `pip install -r requirements.txt`
3. Run the Flask application: `python test_app.py`

## Usage
1. Open a web browser and navigate to `http://localhost:5000`.
2. Upload files using the file upload form.
3. Select the analysis type (plagiarism detection or text similarity analysis).
4. View the results on the web page.

## Contributing
Contributions are welcome! To contribute, please:
1. Fork the repository.
2. Make changes and commit them.
3. Create a pull request.

## License
This project is licensed under the MIT License.

---

## 🧠 How It Works
The system works end-to-end as follows:
1. **User Uploads Files**: The user uploads files through the web interface provided by the Flask application (`test_app.py`).
2. **File Conversion**: If necessary, the files are converted into plain text using the `convert_file_to_txt` function from `utils.file_converter.py`. This step is crucial for preprocessing files before they can be analyzed.
3. **Text Preprocessing**: The converted text is then preprocessed using the `preprocess_text` function from `utils.test_findMatch.py`, which removes punctuation and converts the text to lowercase.
4. **K-gram Generation**: The preprocessed text is then used to generate k-grams using the `generate_kgrams` function from `utils.test_findMatch.py`.
5. **Hashing**: Each k-gram is hashed using the `hash_kgrams` function from `utils.test_findMatch.py`.
6. **Winnowing**: The hashed k-grams are then processed using the winnowing algorithm (`winnow` function from `utils.test_findMatch.py`) to select fingerprints.
7. **Fingerprint Comparison**: The fingerprints are compared across documents using the `compare_fingerprints` function from `utils.test_findMatch.py` to find matches and measure text similarity.
8. **Results**: The results of the analysis are then returned to the user through the web interface.

This process enables the system to efficiently compare documents and detect plagiarism or measure text similarity, providing a useful tool for various applications such as academic integrity verification or content analysis."

```
from flask import Flask, request, jsonify, render_template
from utils.test_findMatch import process_files

from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from utils.test_findMatch import process_files, process_tfidf_files
from utils.file_converter import convert_file_to_txt

test_app = Flask(__name__)


@test_app.route("/")
def index():
    """Render the main HTML page."""
    return render_template("test_index.html")


@test_app.route("/check_plagiarism", methods=["POST"])
def check_plagiarism():
    """API Endpoint to receive files and return plagiarism results."""
    uploaded_files = request.files.getlist("files")

    # Store file contents for highlighting
    file_contents = {}
    for file in uploaded_files:
        file_contents[file.filename] = file.read().decode("utf-8")
        file.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer for processing

    plagiarism_results, common_matches = process_files(uploaded_files)

    # Format results for the frontend
    formatted_results = {}
    file_names = [file.filename for file in uploaded_files]

    for i in range(len(file_names)):
        formatted_results[file_names[i]] = []
        for j in range(len(file_names)):
            if i != j:
                key = f"{i}_{j}"
                if key in plagiarism_results:
                    formatted_results[file_names[i]].append(
                        {
                            "file": file_names[j],
                            "plagiarism": plagiarism_results[key],
                            "matches": common_matches[key],
                        }
                    )
                else:
                    formatted_results[file_names[i]].append(
                        {"file": file_names[j], "plagiarism": 0, "matches": None}
                    )

    return jsonify(
        {
            "results": formatted_results,
            "file_names": file_names,
            "file_contents": file_contents,
        }
    )
@test_app.route('/check_text_similarity', methods=['POST'])
def check_text_similarity():
    uploaded_files = request.files.getlist('files')
    
    if len(uploaded_files) < 2:
        return jsonify({"error": "Please upload at least two text files."}), 400

    # Store file contents (convert to text first)
    file_contents = {}
    valid_files = []
    
    for file in uploaded_files:
        # Convert file to text content
        content = convert_file_to_txt(file)
        
        if content.strip():  # Only process if we got some content
            file_contents[file.filename] = content
            valid_files.append(file)
        else:
            print(f"Warning: No content extracted from {file.filename}")
        
        file.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer

    if len(valid_files) < 2:
        return jsonify({"error": "At least two files must contain readable content."}), 400

    result = process_tfidf_files(valid_files)
    if result is None:

```
### File: utils\file_converter.py
```
import os
import tempfile
from PyPDF2 import PdfReader
from docx import Document

def convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a PDF FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        reader = PdfReader(file_storage.stream)
        text_content = ""
        for page in reader.pages:
            text_content += page.extract_text() + "\n"
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting PDF '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a DOCX FileStorage object to text content.
    """
    try:
        with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=False, suffix='.docx') as temp_file:
            file_storage.save(temp_file.name)
            
        document = Document(temp_file.name)
        text_content = ""
        for paragraph in document.paragraphs:
            text_content += paragraph.text + "\n"
        
        os.unlink(temp_file.name)
        return text_content
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"Error converting DOCX '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
        return ""

def convert_file_to_txt(file_storage):
    """
    Converts a file to text based on its extension.
    """
    filename = file_storage.filename.lower()
    
    if filename.endswith('.pdf'):
        return convert_pdf_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.docx') or filename.endswith('.doc'):
        return convert_docx_to_txt(file_storage)
    elif filename.endswith('.txt'):
        try:
            content = file_storage.read().decode('utf-8')
            file_storage.seek(0)  # Reset file pointer
            return content
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error reading TXT file '{file_storage.filename}': {e}")
            return ""
    else:
        print(f"Unsupported file type: {filename}")
        return ""
```

### File: utils\test_findMatch.py
```
import hashlib
import re
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer
from sklearn.metrics.pairwise import cosine_similarity
from utils.file_converter import convert_file_to_txt


def preprocess_text(text):
    """Preprocess text by removing punctuation and converting to lowercase."""
    text = re.sub(r"[^\w\s]", "", text).lower()
    return text


def generate_kgrams(text, k):
    """Generate k-grams from the text with their positions."""
    kgrams = []
    for i in range(len(text) - k + 1):
        kgrams.append({"text": text[i : i + k], "start": i, "end": i + k})
    return kgrams


def hash_kgrams(kgrams):
    """Hash each k-gram using SHA-256 and keep position info."""
    hashed_kgrams = []
    for kgram in kgrams:
        hash_object = hashlib.sha256(kgram["text"].encode())
        hashed_kgrams.append(
            {
                "hash": int(hash_object.hexdigest(), 16),
                "start": kgram["start"],
                "end": kgram["end"],
            }
        )
    return hashed_kgrams


def winnow(hashed_kgrams, w):
    """Winnowing algorithm to select fingerprints with positions."""
    if not hashed_kgrams or w <= 0:
        return []

    fingerprints = []
    window = [float("inf")] * w
    r = 0
    min_index = 0

    for i, hashed_kgram in enumerate(hashed_kgrams):
        r = i % w
        window[r] = hashed_kgram["hash"]

        if min_index == r:
            # Scan leftward to find new minimum
            min_index = r
            for j in range(r - 1, -1, -1):
                if window[j] < window[min_index]:
                    min_index = j
            for j in range(w - 1, r, -1):
                if window[j] < window[min_index]:
                    min_index = j

            # Ensure we don't go out of bounds
            selected_index = max(0, min(i - (r - min_index), len(hashed_kgrams) - 1))
            fingerprints.append(
                {
                    "hash": window[min_index],
                    "start": hashed_kgrams[selected_index]["start"],
                    "end": hashed_kgrams[selected_index]["end"],
                }
            )
        else:
            # Compare with current minimum and update if necessary
            if window[r] <= window[min_index]:
                min_index = r
                fingerprints.append(
                    {
                        "hash": window[r],
                        "start": hashed_kgram["start"],
                        "end": hashed_kgram["end"],
                    }
                )

    return fingerprints


def compare_fingerprints(fingerprints_list, original_texts):
    """Compare fingerprints across documents and return matches with positions."""
    plagiarism_results = {}
    common_matches = {}

    for i, fingerprints_i in enumerate(fingerprints_list):
        for j, fingerprints_j in enumerate(fingerprints_list):
            if i != j:
                # Convert to sets of hashes for quick lookup
                set_

```", agent="Code Analyst", status="completed", output="### File: test_app.py
The project is a plagiarism detection application built using Python and Flask. It provides a web interface for users to upload files, which are then processed to detect plagiarism. The application can handle various file formats, including PDF, DOCX, and TXT, by converting them into a standard text format for comparison. The core functionality involves preprocessing text, generating k-grams, hashing, and comparing fingerprints across documents to identify potential plagiarism.

## 🧱 System Architecture Overview
The system architecture of the project is modular, with separate modules for handling file conversions, plagiarism detection algorithms, and the web application. The `file_converter.py` module is responsible for converting different file types into plain text, while the `test_findMatch.py` module contains the algorithms for detecting plagiarism. ### File: app.py
```
from dotenv import load_dotenv
load_dotenv()

import re
from fastapi import FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.staticfiles import StaticFiles
from fastapi.responses import FileResponse
from orchestrator import run_pipeline
from summary_agent import build_digest
from ingestion import fetch_articles

app = FastAPI()

app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],
    allow_methods=["GET"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

app.mount("/assets", StaticFiles(directory="frontend"), name="static")


@app.get("/")
def index():
    return FileResponse("frontend/index.html")


@app.get("/api/digest")
def get_digest():
    try:
        outputs = run_pipeline()
        digest  = build_digest(outputs)
        return {
            "status":   "ok",
            "sections": _parse_digest(digest),
            "raw":      digest,
            "agents":   [
                {"domain": o["domain"], "count": o["count"], "bullets": o["bullets"]}
                for o in outputs
            ],
        }
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "message": str(e)}


@app.get("/api/articles/{domain}")
def get_articles(domain: str):
    if domain not in ("tech", "finance", "sports"):
        return {"status": "error", "message": "Invalid domain. Use: tech, finance, sports"}
    try:
        articles = fetch_articles(domain)
        return {"status": "ok", "domain": domain, "count": len(articles), "articles": articles}
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "message": str(e)}


def _parse_digest(text: str) -> dict:
    result  = {}
    pattern = re.split(r"(🔥 Top Headlines|🧠 Tech|💰 Finance|⚽ Sports)", text)
    for i in range(1, len(pattern), 2):
        key     = pattern[i].strip()
        content = pattern[i + 1].strip() if i + 1 < len(pattern) else ""
        bullets = [
            b.lstrip("- ").strip()
            for b in content.splitlines()
            if b.strip().startswith("-")
        ]
        result[key] = bullets
    return result
```

### File: ingestion.py
```
import os
import requests
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
from datetime import datetime, timezone

NEWS_API_KEY = os.getenv("NEWS_API_KEY")
NEWS_API_URL = "https://newsapi.org/v2/top-headlines"

# RSS feed sources per domain (BBC, Reuters)
RSS_FEEDS = {
    "tech": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/news/technology/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/technologyNews",
    ],
    "finance": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/news/business/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/businessNews",
    ],
    "sports": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/sport/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/sportsNews",
    ],
}

NEWSAPI_CATEGORIES = {
    "tech":    "technology",
    "finance": "business",
    "sports":  "sports",
}


def fetch_articles(domain: str, page_size: int = 8) -> list[dict]:
    articles = []
    articles.extend(_fetch_rss(domain))
    articles.extend(_fetch_newsapi(domain, page_size))
    # deduplicate by title at ingestion level
    seen, unique = set(), []
    for a in articles:
        key = a["title"].lower().strip()
        if key not in seen:
            seen.add(key)
            unique.append(a)
    return unique


def _fetch_newsapi(domain: str, page_size: int) -> list[dict]:
    if not NEWS_API_KEY:
        return []
    try:
        params = {
            "apiKey":   NEWS_API_KEY,
            "language": "en",
            "pageSize": page_size,
            "category": NEWSAPI_CATEGORIES[domain],
        }
        resp = requests.get(NEWS_API_URL, params=params, timeout=10)
        resp.raise_for_status()
        raw_list = resp.json().get("articles", [])
        return [
            _normalize(
                title=a["title"],
                content=a.get("description") or a.get("content", ""),
                source=a.get("source", {}).get("name", "NewsAPI"),
                published_at=a.get("publishedAt", _now()),
                category_hint=domain,
            )
            for a in raw_list
            if a.get("title") and a.get("description")
        ]
    except Exception:
        return []


def _fetch_rss(domain: str) -> list[dict]:
    articles = []
    for url in RSS_FEEDS[domain]:
        try:
            resp = requests.get(url, timeout=10, headers={"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"})
            resp.raise_for_status()
            root = ET.fromstring(resp.content)
            for item in root.findall(".//item")[:8]:
                title   = item.findtext("title", "").strip()
                content = item.findtext("description", "").strip()
                source  = item.findtext("source", url.split("/")[2])
                pub     = item.findtext("pubDate", _now())
                if title and content:
                    articles.append(_normalize(title, content, source, pub, domain))
        except Exception:
            continue
    return articles


def _normalize(title: str, content: str, source: str, published_at: str, category_hint: str) -> dict:
    return

```
### File: orchestrator.py
```
import time
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed
from ingestion import fetch_articles
from agents import run_agent

DOMAINS  = ["tech", "finance", "sports"]
MAX_RETRIES = 2


def run_pipeline() -> list[dict]:
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=len(DOMAINS)) as executor:
        futures = {
            executor.submit(_fetch_and_run_with_retry, domain): domain
            for domain in DOMAINS
        }
        results = {}
        for future in as_completed(futures):
            domain = futures[future]
            try:
                results[domain] = future.result()
            except Exception as e:
                results[domain] = {
                    "domain":  domain,
                    "bullets": [f"Pipeline error: {e}"],
                    "summary": f"- Pipeline error: {e}",
                    "count":   0,
                }

    # return in consistent order
    return [results[d] for d in DOMAINS]


def _fetch_and_run_with_retry(domain: str) -> dict:
    last_error = None
    for attempt in range(1, MAX_RETRIES + 1):
        try:
            articles = fetch_articles(domain)
            return run_agent(domain, articles)
        except Exception as e:
            last_error = e
            if attempt < MAX_RETRIES:
                time.sleep(2 ** attempt)  # exponential backoff
    raise last_error
```

### File: README.md
```
# 📡 AI News Digest — Multi-Agent News Pipeline

AI News Digest is an intelligent news briefing system powered by a multi-agent AI pipeline. It automatically collects real-time news from RSS feeds (BBC, Reuters) and NewsAPI across three domains — Technology, Finance, and Sports — then routes each domain through a specialized AI agent that filters, deduplicates, and summarizes the articles. A final Summary Agent merges all outputs, ranks the top stories by global impact, and delivers a clean daily briefing through a modern web dashboard.

## Tech Stack

| Layer | Technology |
|---|---|
| Backend | FastAPI, Uvicorn |
| LLM | LLaMA 3.3 70B via Groq (free) |
| News Sources | NewsAPI, BBC RSS, Reuters RSS |
| Agent Pipeline | Custom multi-agent (Filter → Chunk → Summarize → Deduplicate → Output) |
| Frontend | HTML, CSS, JavaScript |

## Setup

1. Clone the repo
   ```bash
   git clone https://github.com/rbbhadiyar/AI-News-Digest.git
   cd AI-News-Digest
   ```

2. Install dependencies
   ```bash
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

3. Create `.env` from the example
   ```bash
   cp .env.example .env
   ```
   Fill in your API keys inside `.env`:
   - **GROQ_API_KEY** → [console.groq.com](https://console.groq.com) (free)
   - **NEWS_API_KEY** → [newsapi.org](https://newsapi.org) (free tier)

4. Run
   ```bash
   python main.py
   ```

5. Open [http://localhost:8000](http://localhost:8000)

---

```
### File: summary_agent.py
```
import os
from groq import Groq

client = Groq(api_key=os.getenv("GROQ_API_KEY"))
MODEL = "llama-3.3-70b-versatile"

SYSTEM_PROMPT = """You are a Chief News Editor producing a daily briefing.

You receive bullet-point summaries from three specialist analysts: Tech, Finance, and Sports.

Your tasks:
1. Top Headlines: Pick the 3 most globally important stories across ALL domains. Rank by real-world impact.
2. Remove redundancy: If the same story appears in multiple sections, keep it only in Top Headlines.
3. Present each domain section cleanly with the bullets provided, removing any duplicates.
4. Keep each bullet concise (one sentence max).

Output STRICTLY in this format (use these exact emoji headers):

🔥 Top Headlines
- <most important story>
- <second most important>
- <third most important>

🧠 Tech
- <bullet>
- <bullet>

💰 Finance
- <bullet>
- <bullet>

⚽ Sports
- <bullet>
- <bullet>"""

DOMAIN_LABELS = {
    "tech":    "🧠 Tech",
    "finance": "💰 Finance",
    "sports":  "⚽ Sports",
}


def build_digest(agent_outputs: list[dict]) -> str:
    combined = "\n\n".join(
        f"{DOMAIN_LABELS.get(o['domain'], o['domain'])}:\n{o['summary']}"
        for o in agent_outputs
    )

    response = client.chat.completions.create(
        model=MODEL,
        messages=[
            {"role": "system", "content": SYSTEM_PROMPT},
            {"role": "user",   "content": combined},
        ],
        temperature=0.2,
    )

    return response.choices[0].message.content.strip()
```

### File: frontend\app.js
```
const SECTIONS_META = {
  "🔥 Top Headlines": { icon: "🔥", badge: "HOT",     badgeClass: "badge-hot",     cardClass: "card-top" },
  "🧠 Tech":          { icon: "🧠", badge: "TECH",    badgeClass: "badge-tech",    cardClass: "" },
  "💰 Finance":       { icon: "💰", badge: "FINANCE", badgeClass: "badge-finance", cardClass: "" },
  "⚽ Sports":        { icon: "⚽", badge: "SPORTS",  badgeClass: "badge-sports",  cardClass: "" },
};

function setLoading(on) {
  const btn = document.getElementById("refresh-btn");
  const bar = document.getElementById("status-bar");
  btn.disabled = on;
  document.getElementById("btn-icon").textContent = on ? "⏳" : "⚡";
  bar.classList.toggle("visible", on);
}

function showError(msg) {
  const box = document.getElementById("error-box");
  box.textContent = "⚠️ " + msg;
  box.classList.add("visible");
}

function clearError() {
  document.getElementById("error-box").classList.remove("visible");
}

function renderSkeletons() {
  const grid = document.getElementById("digest-grid");
  grid.innerHTML = Array.from({ length: 4 }, () => `
    <div class="skeleton-card">
      <div class="skeleton-line short" style="margin-bottom:18px"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line long"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line medium"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line long"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line medium"></div>
    </div>
  `).join("");
}

function renderDigest(sections) {
  const grid = document.getElementById("digest-grid");
  grid.innerHTML = "";

  const order = ["🔥 Top Headlines", "🧠 Tech", "💰 Finance", "⚽ Sports"];

  order.forEach(key => {
    const bullets = sections[key];
    if (!bullets || bullets.length === 0) return;

    const meta = SECTIONS_META[key] || { icon: "📰", badge: key, badgeClass: "", cardClass: "" };
    const li = bullets.map(b => `<li>${b}</li>`).join("");

    const card = document.createElement("div");
    card.className = `card ${meta.cardClass}`;
    card.innerHTML = `
      <div class="card-header">
        <span class="card-icon">${meta.icon}</span>
        <span class="card-title">${key}</span>
        <span class="card-badge ${meta.badgeClass}">${meta.badge}</span>
      </div>
      <ul class="bullet-list">${li}</ul>
    `;
    grid.appendChild(card);
  });

  document.getElementById("last-updated").textContent =
    "Last updated: " + new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
}

async function loadDigest() {
  clearError();
  setLoading(true);
  renderSkeletons();

  try {
    const res = await fetch("/api/digest");
    const data = await res.json();

    if (data.status === "error") {
      showError(data.message);
      document.getElementById("digest-grid").innerHTML = "";
      return;
    }

    renderDigest(data.sections);
  } catch (e) {
    showError("Could not reach the server. Make sure the backend is running.");
    document.getElementById("digest-grid").innerHTML = "";
  } finally {
    setLoading(false);
  }

```
### File: app.py
```
from dotenv import load_dotenv
load_dotenv()

import re
from fastapi import FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.staticfiles import StaticFiles
from fastapi.responses import FileResponse
from orchestrator import run_pipeline
from summary_agent import build_digest
from ingestion import fetch_articles

app = FastAPI()

app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],
    allow_methods=["GET"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

app.mount("/assets", StaticFiles(directory="frontend"), name="static")


@app.get("/")
def index():
    return FileResponse("frontend/index.html")


@app.get("/api/digest")
def get_digest():
    try:
        outputs = run_pipeline()
        digest  = build_digest(outputs)
        return {
            "status":   "ok",
            "sections": _parse_digest(digest),
            "raw":      digest,
            "agents":   [
                {"domain": o["domain"], "count": o["count"], "bullets": o["bullets"]}
                for o in outputs
            ],
        }
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "message": str(e)}


@app.get("/api/articles/{domain}")
def get_articles(domain: str):
    if domain not in ("tech", "finance", "sports"):
        return {"status": "error", "message": "Invalid domain. Use: tech, finance, sports"}
    try:
        articles = fetch_articles(domain)
        return {"status": "ok", "domain": domain, "count": len(articles), "articles": articles}
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "message": str(e)}


def _parse_digest(text: str) -> dict:
    result  = {}
    pattern = re.split(r"(🔥 Top Headlines|🧠 Tech|💰 Finance|⚽ Sports)", text)
    for i in range(1, len(pattern), 2):
        key     = pattern[i].strip()
        content = pattern[i + 1].strip() if i + 1 < len(pattern) else ""
        bullets = [
            b.lstrip("- ").strip()
            for b in content.splitlines()
            if b.strip().startswith("-")
        ]
        result[key] = bullets
    return result
```

### File: ingestion.py
```
import os
import requests
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
from datetime import datetime, timezone

NEWS_API_KEY = os.getenv("NEWS_API_KEY")
NEWS_API_URL = "https://newsapi.org/v2/top-headlines"

# RSS feed sources per domain (BBC, Reuters)
RSS_FEEDS = {
    "tech": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/news/technology/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/technologyNews",
    ],
    "finance": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/news/business/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/businessNews",
    ],
    "sports": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/sport/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/sportsNews",
    ],
}

NEWSAPI_CATEGORIES = {
    "tech":    "technology",
    "finance": "business",
    "sports":  "sports",
}


def fetch_articles(domain: str, page_size: int = 8) -> list[dict]:
    articles = []
    articles.extend(_fetch_rss(domain))
    articles.extend(_fetch_newsapi(domain, page_size))
    # deduplicate by title at ingestion level
    seen, unique = set(), []
    for a in articles:
        key = a["title"].lower().strip()
        if key not in seen:
            seen.add(key)
            unique.append(a)
    return unique


def _fetch_newsapi(domain: str, page_size: int) -> list[dict]:
    if not NEWS_API_KEY:
        return []
    try:
        params = {
            "apiKey":   NEWS_API_KEY,
            "language": "en",
            "pageSize": page_size,
            "category": NEWSAPI_CATEGORIES[domain],
        }
        resp = requests.get(NEWS_API_URL, params=params, timeout=10)
        resp.raise_for_status()
        raw_list = resp.json().get("articles", [])
        return [
            _normalize(
                title=a["title"],
                content=a.get("description") or a.get("content", ""),
                source=a.get("source", {}).get("name", "NewsAPI"),
                published_at=a.get("publishedAt", _now()),
                category_hint=domain,
            )
            for a in raw_list
            if a.get("title") and a.get("description")
        ]
    except Exception:
        return []


def _fetch_rss(domain: str) -> list[dict]:
    articles = []
    for url in RSS_FEEDS[domain]:
        try:
            resp = requests.get(url, timeout=10, headers={"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"})
            resp.raise_for_status()
            root = ET.fromstring(resp.content)
            for item in root.findall(".//item")[:8]:
                title   = item.findtext("title", "").strip()
                content = item.findtext("description", "").strip()
                source  = item.findtext("source", url.split("/")[2])
                pub     = item.findtext("pubDate", _now())
                if title and content:
                    articles.append(_normalize(title, content, source, pub, domain))
        except Exception:
            continue
    return articles


def _normalize(title: str, content: str, source: str, published_at: str, category_hint: str) -> dict:
    return
```

### File: orchestrator.py
```
import time
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed
from ingestion import fetch_articles
from agents import run_agent

DOMAINS  = ["tech", "finance", "sports"]
MAX_RETRIES = 2


def run_pipeline() -> list[dict]:
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=len(DOMAINS)) as executor:
        futures = {
            executor.submit(_fetch_and_run_with_retry, domain): domain
            for domain in DOMAINS
        }
        results = {}
        for future in as_completed(futures):
            domain = futures[future]
            try:
                results[domain] = future.result()
            except Exception as e:
                results[domain] = {
                    "domain":  domain,
                    "bullets": [f"Pipeline error: {e}"],
                    "summary": f"- Pipeline error: {e}",
                    "count":   0,
                }

    # return in consistent order
    return [results[d] for d in DOMAINS]


def _fetch_and_run_with_retry(domain: str) -> dict:
    last_error = None
    for attempt in range(1, MAX_RETRIES + 1):
        try:
            articles = fetch_articles(domain)
            return run_agent(domain, articles)
        except Exception as e:
            last_error = e
            if attempt < MAX_RETRIES:
                time.sleep(2 ** attempt)  # exponential backoff
    raise last_error
```

### File: README.md
```
# 📡 AI News Digest — Multi-Agent News Pipeline

AI News Digest is an intelligent news briefing system powered by a multi-agent AI pipeline. It automatically collects real-time news from RSS feeds (BBC, Reuters) and NewsAPI across three domains — Technology, Finance, and Sports — then routes each domain through a specialized AI agent that filters, deduplicates, and summarizes the articles. A final Summary Agent merges all outputs, ranks the top stories by global impact, and delivers a clean daily briefing through a modern web dashboard.

## Tech Stack

| Layer | Technology |
|---|---|
| Backend | FastAPI, Uvicorn |
| LLM | LLaMA 3.3 70B via Groq (free) |
| News Sources | NewsAPI, BBC RSS, Reuters RSS |
| Agent Pipeline | Custom multi-agent (Filter → Chunk → Summarize → Deduplicate → Output) |
| Frontend | HTML, CSS, JavaScript |

## Setup

1. Clone the repo
   ```bash
   git clone https://github.com/rbbhadiyar/AI-News-Digest.git
   cd AI-News-Digest
   ```

2. Install dependencies
   ```bash
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

3. Create `.env` from the example
   ```bash
   cp .env.example .env
   ```
   Fill in your API keys inside `.env`:
   - **GROQ_API_KEY** → [console.groq.com](https://console.groq.com) (free)
   - **NEWS_API_KEY** → [newsapi.org](https://newsapi.org) (free tier)

4. Run
   ```bash
   python main.py
   ```

5. Open [http://localhost:8000](http://localhost:8000)

---

```
### File: summary_agent.py
```
import os
from groq import Groq

client = Groq(api_key=os.getenv("GROQ_API_KEY"))
MODEL = "llama-3.3-70b-versatile"

SYSTEM_PROMPT = """You are a Chief News Editor producing a daily briefing.

You receive bullet-point summaries from three specialist analysts: Tech, Finance, and Sports.

Your tasks:
1. Top Headlines: Pick the 3 most globally important stories across ALL domains. Rank by real-world impact.
2. Remove redundancy: If the same story appears in multiple sections, keep it only in Top Headlines.
3. Present each domain section cleanly with the bullets provided, removing any duplicates.
4. Keep each bullet concise (one sentence max).

Output STRICTLY in this format (use these exact emoji headers):

🔥 Top Headlines
- <most important story>
- <second most important>
- <third most important>

🧠 Tech
- <bullet>
- <bullet>

💰 Finance
- <bullet>
- <bullet>

⚽ Sports
- <bullet>
- <bullet>"""

DOMAIN_LABELS = {
    "tech":    "🧠 Tech",
    "finance": "💰 Finance",
    "sports":  "⚽ Sports",
}


def build_digest(agent_outputs: list[dict]) -> str:
    combined = "\n\n".join(
        f"{DOMAIN_LABELS.get(o['domain'], o['domain'])}:\n{o['summary']}"
        for o in agent_outputs
    )

    response = client.chat.completions.create(
        model=MODEL,
        messages=[
            {"role": "system", "content": SYSTEM_PROMPT},
            {"role": "user",   "content": combined},
        ],
        temperature=0.2,
    )

    return response.choices[0].message.content.strip()
```

### File: frontend\app.js
```
const SECTIONS_META = {
  "🔥 Top Headlines": { icon: "🔥", badge: "HOT",     badgeClass: "badge-hot",     cardClass: "card-top" },
  "🧠 Tech":          { icon: "🧠", badge: "TECH",    badgeClass: "badge-tech",    cardClass: "" },
  "💰 Finance":       { icon: "💰", badge: "FINANCE", badgeClass: "badge-finance", cardClass: "" },
  "⚽ Sports":        { icon: "⚽", badge: "SPORTS",  badgeClass: "badge-sports",  cardClass: "" },
};

function setLoading(on) {
  const btn = document.getElementById("refresh-btn");
  const bar = document.getElementById("status-bar");
  btn.disabled = on;
  document.getElementById("btn-icon").textContent = on ? "⏳" : "⚡";
  bar.classList.toggle("visible", on);
}

function showError(msg) {
  const box = document.getElementById("error-box");
  box.textContent = "⚠️ " + msg;
  box.classList.add("visible");
}

function clearError() {
  document.getElementById("error-box").classList.remove("visible");
}

function renderSkeletons() {
  const grid = document.getElementById("digest-grid");
  grid.innerHTML = Array.from({ length: 4 }, () => `
    <div class="skeleton-card">
      <div class="skeleton-line short" style="margin-bottom:18px"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line long"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line medium"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line long"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line medium"></div>
    </div>
  `).join("");
}

function renderDigest(sections) {
  const grid = document.getElementById("digest-grid");
  grid.innerHTML = "";

  const order = ["🔥 Top Headlines", "🧠 Tech", "💰 Finance", "⚽ Sports"];

  order.forEach(key => {
    const bullets = sections[key];
    if (!bullets || bullets.length === 0) return;

    const meta = SECTIONS_META[key] || { icon: "📰", badge: key, badgeClass: "", cardClass: "" };
    const li = bullets.map(b => `<li>${b}</li>`).join("");

    const card = document.createElement("div");
    card.className = `card ${meta.cardClass}`;
    card.innerHTML = `
      <div class="card-header">
        <span class="card-icon">${meta.icon}</span>
        <span class="card-title">${key}</span>
        <span class="card-badge ${meta.badgeClass}">${meta.badge}</span>
      </div>
      <ul class="bullet-list">${li}</ul>
    `;
    grid.appendChild(card);
  });

  document.getElementById("last-updated").textContent =
    "Last updated: " + new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
}

async function loadDigest() {
  clearError();
  setLoading(true);
  renderSkeletons();

  try {
    const res = await fetch("/api/digest");
    const data = await res.json();

    if (data.status === "error") {
      showError(data.message);
      document.getElementById("digest-grid").innerHTML = "";
      return;
    }

    renderDigest(data.sections);
  } catch (e) {
    showError("Could not reach the server. Make sure the backend is running.");
    document.getElementById("digest-grid").innerHTML = "";
  } finally {
    setLoading(false);
  }
}

```", agent="Code Analyst", status="completed", output="### File: agents.py
## 🧱 System Architecture Overview
The system architecture can be described as a layered architecture, with each layer having distinct responsibilities and interactions with adjacent layers. The layers include:
- **Presentation Layer**: This layer is responsible for rendering the user interface and handling user interactions. It includes the `frontend/app.js` file, which contains the logic for rendering the news digest.
- **Application Layer**: This layer contains the core application logic, including the `app.py` file, which defines the FastAPI application and endpoints for fetching articles and generating the digest.
- **Business Logic Layer**: This layer is responsible for the processing and orchestration of news articles. It includes files like `ingestion.py`, `orchestrator.py`, `agents.py`, and `summary_agent.py`, which handle data ingestion, pipeline management, and article processing.
- **Data Access Layer**: This layer is responsible for interacting with external data sources, such as RSS feeds and NewsAPI. It is primarily handled by the `ingestion.py` file.

The overall architectural style of the project is a microservices architecture, with each component (ingestion, orchestrator, agents) acting as a separate service that communicates with others to achieve the overall goal. Design patterns used in the project include the Repository pattern for data access and the Factory pattern for creating agents.

## 📂 Folder-by-Folder Explanation
- **Root Directory**: This is the main directory of the project, containing key files like `app.py`, `ingestion.py`, `orchestrator.py`, and `main.py`.
  - `app.py`: Defines the FastAPI application and endpoints.
  - `ingestion.py`: Handles data ingestion from RSS feeds and NewsAPI.
  - `orchestrator.py`: Manages the pipeline for generating the news digest.
  - `main.py`: Serves as the entry point for running the application.
- **frontend Directory**: This directory contains the frontend logic for rendering the news digest.
  - `app.js`: Contains the logic for rendering the news digest and fetching data from the backend.
- **agents Directory**: This directory would contain additional agent files if the project were to be expanded to include more domain-specific agents.

The separation of these directories exists architecturally to maintain a clear distinction between the backend logic, frontend logic, and potential future expansions.

## ⚙️ Key Modules Breakdown
1. **app.py**:
   - Purpose: Defines the FastAPI application and endpoints.
   - Key Functions/Classes: `app`, `get_digest`, `get_articles`, `_parse_digest`.
   - Inputs/Outputs: Accepts HTTP requests, returns JSON responses.
   - Internal Logic: Defines the API endpoints and handles requests.
   - Dependencies: Depends on `ingestion.py` and `orchestrator.py` for data processing.
   - Role in System: Central to the project, defines the API endpoints.
2. **ingestion.py**:
   - Purpose: Handles data ingestion from RSS feeds and NewsAPI.
   - Key Functions/Classes: `fetch_articles`, `_fetch_newsapi`, `_fetch_rss`, `_normalize`.
   - Inputs/Outputs: Accepts domain parameters, returns a list of articles.
   - Internal Logic: Fetches articles from various sources and normalizes them.
   - Dependencies: None.
   - Role in System: Critical for collecting raw data.
3. **orchestrator.py**:
   - Purpose: Manages the pipeline for generating the news digest.
   - Key Functions/Classes: `run_pipeline`, `_fetch_and_run_with_retry`.
   - Inputs/Outputs: Accepts no parameters, returns the generated digest.
   - Internal Logic: Coordinates the pipeline, including data ingestion and agent processing.
   - Dependencies: Depends on `ingestion.py` and `agents.py`.
   - Role in System: Vital for coordinating the different components.

## 🔄 Data Flow Explanation
1. **User Request**: A user requests the news digest through the frontend.
2. **Backend Request**: The frontend sends a request to the backend `app.py` to generate the digest.
3. **Ingestion**: The `app.py` triggers the `ingestion.py` to fetch articles from various sources.
4. **Article Processing**: The fetched articles are processed by domain-specific agents defined in `agents.py`.
5. **Summarization**: The outputs from the agents are summarized by the `summary_agent.py`.
6. **Digest Generation**: The final digest is generated and returned to the frontend.
7. **Rendering**: The frontend renders the digest to the user.

Error paths include handling failures in data ingestion, agent processing, and summarization, with retry logic implemented in the orchestrator.
```

```
### File: app.py
```
from dotenv import load_dotenv
load_dotenv()

import re
from fastapi import FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.staticfiles import StaticFiles
from fastapi.responses import FileResponse
from orchestrator import run_pipeline
from summary_agent import build_digest
from ingestion import fetch_articles

app = FastAPI()

app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],
    allow_methods=["GET"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

app.mount("/assets", StaticFiles(directory="frontend"), name="static")


@app.get("/")
def index():
    return FileResponse("frontend/index.html")


@app.get("/api/digest")
def get_digest():
    try:
        outputs = run_pipeline()
        digest  = build_digest(outputs)
        return {
            "status":   "ok",
            "sections": _parse_digest(digest),
            "raw":      digest,
            "agents":   [
                {"domain": o["domain"], "count": o["count"], "bullets": o["bullets"]}
                for o in outputs
            ],
        }
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "message": str(e)}


@app.get("/api/articles/{domain}")
def get_articles(domain: str):
    if domain not in ("tech", "finance", "sports"):
        return {"status": "error", "message": "Invalid domain. Use: tech, finance, sports"}
    try:
        articles = fetch_articles(domain)
        return {"status": "ok", "domain": domain, "count": len(articles), "articles": articles}
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "message": str(e)}


def _parse_digest(text: str) -> dict:
    result  = {}
    pattern = re.split(r"(🔥 Top Headlines|🧠 Tech|💰 Finance|⚽ Sports)", text)
    for i in range(1, len(pattern), 2):
        key     = pattern[i].strip()
        content = pattern[i + 1].strip() if i + 1 < len(pattern) else ""
        bullets = [
            b.lstrip("- ").strip()
            for b in content.splitlines()
            if b.strip().startswith("-")
        ]
        result[key] = bullets
    return result
```

### File: ingestion.py
```
import os
import requests
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
from datetime import datetime, timezone

NEWS_API_KEY = os.getenv("NEWS_API_KEY")
NEWS_API_URL = "https://newsapi.org/v2/top-headlines"

# RSS feed sources per domain (BBC, Reuters)
RSS_FEEDS = {
    "tech": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/news/technology/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/technologyNews",
    ],
    "finance": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/news/business/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/businessNews",
    ],
    "sports": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/sport/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/sportsNews",
    ],
}

NEWSAPI_CATEGORIES = {
    "tech":    "technology",
    "finance": "business",
    "sports":  "sports",
}


def fetch_articles(domain: str, page_size: int = 8) -> list[dict]:
    articles = []
    articles.extend(_fetch_rss(domain))
    articles.extend(_fetch_newsapi(domain, page_size))
    # deduplicate by title at ingestion level
    seen, unique = set(), []
    for a in articles:
        key = a["title"].lower().strip()
        if key not in seen:
            seen.add(key)
            unique.append(a)
    return unique


def _fetch_newsapi(domain: str, page_size: int) -> list[dict]:
    if not NEWS_API_KEY:
        return []
    try:
        params = {
            "apiKey":   NEWS_API_KEY,
            "language": "en",
            "pageSize": page_size,
            "category": NEWSAPI_CATEGORIES[domain],
        }
        resp = requests.get(NEWS_API_URL, params=params, timeout=10)
        resp.raise_for_status()
        raw_list = resp.json().get("articles", [])
        return [
            _normalize(
                title=a["title"],
                content=a.get("description") or a.get("content", ""),
                source=a.get("source", {}).get("name", "NewsAPI"),
                published_at=a.get("publishedAt", _now()),
                category_hint=domain,
            )
            for a in raw_list
            if a.get("title") and a.get("description")
        ]
    except Exception:
        return []


def _fetch_rss(domain: str) -> list[dict]:
    articles = []
    for url in RSS_FEEDS[domain]:
        try:
            resp = requests.get(url, timeout=10, headers={"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"})
            resp.raise_for_status()
            root = ET.fromstring(resp.content)
            for item in root.findall(".//item")[:8]:
                title   = item.findtext("title", "").strip()
                content = item.findtext("description", "").strip()
                source  = item.findtext("source", url.split("/")[2])
                pub     = item.findtext("pubDate", _now())
                if title and content:
                    articles.append(_normalize(title, content, source, pub, domain))
        except Exception:
            continue
    return articles


def _normalize(title: str, content: str, source: str, published_at: str, category_hint: str) -> dict:
    return
```

### File: orchestrator.py
```
import time
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed
from ingestion import fetch_articles
from agents import run_agent

DOMAINS  = ["tech", "finance", "sports"]
MAX_RETRIES = 2


def run_pipeline() -> list[dict]:
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=len(DOMAINS)) as executor:
        futures = {
            executor.submit(_fetch_and_run_with_retry, domain): domain
            for domain in DOMAINS
        }
        results = {}
        for future in as_completed(futures):
            domain = futures[future]
            try:
                results[domain] = future.result()
            except Exception as e:
                results[domain] = {
                    "domain":  domain,
                    "bullets": [f"Pipeline error: {e}"],
                    "summary": f"- Pipeline error: {e}",
                    "count":   0,
                }

    # return in consistent order
    return [results[d] for d in DOMAINS]


def _fetch_and_run_with_retry(domain: str) -> dict:
    last_error = None
    for attempt in range(1, MAX_RETRIES + 1):
        try:
            articles = fetch_articles(domain)
            return run_agent(domain, articles)
        except Exception as e:
            last_error = e
            if attempt < MAX_RETRIES:
                time.sleep(2 ** attempt)  # exponential backoff
    raise last_error
```

### File: README.md
```
# 📡 AI News Digest — Multi-Agent News Pipeline

AI News Digest is an intelligent news briefing system powered by a multi-agent AI pipeline. It automatically collects real-time news from RSS feeds (BBC, Reuters) and NewsAPI across three domains — Technology, Finance, and Sports — then routes each domain through a specialized AI agent that filters, deduplicates, and summarizes the articles. A final Summary Agent merges all outputs, ranks the top stories by global impact, and delivers a clean daily briefing through a modern web dashboard.

## Tech Stack

| Layer | Technology |
|---|---|
| Backend | FastAPI, Uvicorn |
| LLM | LLaMA 3.3 70B via Groq (free) |
| News Sources | NewsAPI, BBC RSS, Reuters RSS |
| Agent Pipeline | Custom multi-agent (Filter → Chunk → Summarize → Deduplicate → Output) |
| Frontend | HTML, CSS, JavaScript |

## Setup

1. Clone the repo
   ```bash
   git clone https://github.com/rbbhadiyar/AI-News-Digest.git
   cd AI-News-Digest
   ```

2. Install dependencies
   ```bash
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

3. Create `.env` from the example
   ```bash
   cp .env.example .env
   ```
   Fill in your API keys inside `.env`:
   - **GROQ_API_KEY** → [console.groq.com](https://console.groq.com) (free)
   - **NEWS_API_KEY** → [newsapi.org](https://newsapi.org) (free tier)

4. Run
   ```bash
   python main.py
   ```

5. Open [http://localhost:8000](http://localhost:8000)

```
### File: summary_agent.py
```
import os
from groq import Groq

client = Groq(api_key=os.getenv("GROQ_API_KEY"))
MODEL = "llama-3.3-70b-versatile"

SYSTEM_PROMPT = """You are a Chief News Editor producing a daily briefing.

You receive bullet-point summaries from three specialist analysts: Tech, Finance, and Sports.

Your tasks:
1. Top Headlines: Pick the 3 most globally important stories across ALL domains. Rank by real-world impact.
2. Remove redundancy: If the same story appears in multiple sections, keep it only in Top Headlines.
3. Present each domain section cleanly with the bullets provided, removing any duplicates.
4. Keep each bullet concise (one sentence max).

Output STRICTLY in this format (use these exact emoji headers):

🔥 Top Headlines
- <most important story>
- <second most important>
- <third most important>

🧠 Tech
- <bullet>
- <bullet>

💰 Finance
- <bullet>
- <bullet>

⚽ Sports
- <bullet>
- <bullet>"""

DOMAIN_LABELS = {
    "tech":    "🧠 Tech",
    "finance": "💰 Finance",
    "sports":  "⚽ Sports",
}


def build_digest(agent_outputs: list[dict]) -> str:
    combined = "\n\n".join(
        f"{DOMAIN_LABELS.get(o['domain'], o['domain'])}:\n{o['summary']}"
        for o in agent_outputs
    )

    response = client.chat.completions.create(
        model=MODEL,
        messages=[
            {"role": "system", "content": SYSTEM_PROMPT},
            {"role": "user",   "content": combined},
        ],
        temperature=0.2,
    )

    return response.choices[0].message.content.strip()

const SECTIONS_META = {
  "🔥 Top Headlines": { icon: "🔥", badge: "HOT",     badgeClass: "badge-hot",     cardClass: "card-top" },
  "🧠 Tech":          { icon: "🧠", badge: "TECH",    badgeClass: "badge-tech",    cardClass: "" },
  "💰 Finance":       { icon: "💰", badge: "FINANCE", badgeClass: "badge-finance", cardClass: "" },
  "⚽ Sports":        { icon: "⚽", badge: "SPORTS",  badgeClass: "badge-sports",  cardClass: "" },
};

function setLoading(on) {
  const btn = document.getElementById("refresh-btn");
  const bar = document.getElementById("status-bar");
  btn.disabled = on;
  document.getElementById("btn-icon").textContent = on ? "⏳" : "⚡";
  bar.classList.toggle("visible", on);
}

function showError(msg) {
  const box = document.getElementById("error-box");
  box.textContent = "⚠️ " + msg;
  box.classList.add("visible");
}

function clearError() {
  document.getElementById("error-box").classList.remove("visible");
}

function renderSkeletons() {
  const grid = document.getElementById("digest-grid");
  grid.innerHTML = Array.from({ length: 4 }, () => `
    <div class="skeleton-card">
      <div class="skeleton-line short" style="margin-bottom:18px"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line long"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line medium"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line long"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line medium"></div>
    </div>
  `).join("");
}

function renderDigest(sections) {
  const grid = document.getElementById("digest-grid");
  grid.innerHTML = "";

  const order = ["🔥 Top Headlines", "🧠 Tech", "💰 Finance", "⚽ Sports"];

  order.forEach(key => {
    const bullets = sections[key];
    if (!bullets || bullets.length === 0) return;

    const meta = SECTIONS_META[key] || { icon: "📰", badge: key, badgeClass: "", cardClass: "" };
    const li = bullets.map(b => `<li>${b}</li>`).join("");

    const card = document.createElement("div");
    card.className = `card ${meta.cardClass}`;
    card.innerHTML = `
      <div class="card-header">
        <span class="card-icon">${meta.icon}</span>
        <span class="card-title">${key}</span>
        <span class="card-badge ${meta.badgeClass}">${meta.badge}</span>
      </div>
      <ul class="bullet-list">${li}</ul>
    `;
    grid.appendChild(card);
  });

  document.getElementById("last-updated").textContent =
    "Last updated: " + new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
}

async function loadDigest() {
  clearError();
  setLoading(true);
  renderSkeletons();

  try {
    const res = await fetch("/api/digest");
    const data = await res.json();

    if (data.status === "error") {
      showError(data.message);
      document.getElementById("digest-grid").innerHTML = "";
      return;
    }

    renderDigest(data.sections);
  } catch (e) {
    showError("Could not reach the server. Make sure the backend is running.");
    document.getElementById("digest-grid").innerHTML = "";
  } finally {
    setLoading(false);
  }
}

```
### File: app.py
```
from dotenv import load_dotenv
load_dotenv()

import re
from fastapi import FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.staticfiles import StaticFiles
from fastapi.responses import FileResponse
from orchestrator import run_pipeline
from summary_agent import build_digest
from ingestion import fetch_articles

app = FastAPI()

app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],
    allow_methods=["GET"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

app.mount("/assets", StaticFiles(directory="frontend"), name="static")


@app.get("/")
def index():
    return FileResponse("frontend/index.html")


@app.get("/api/digest")
def get_digest():
    try:
        outputs = run_pipeline()
        digest  = build_digest(outputs)
        return {
            "status":   "ok",
            "sections": _parse_digest(digest),
            "raw":      digest,
            "agents":   [
                {"domain": o["domain"], "count": o["count"], "bullets": o["bullets"]}
                for o in outputs
            ],
        }
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "message": str(e)}


@app.get("/api/articles/{domain}")
def get_articles(domain: str):
    if domain not in ("tech", "finance", "sports"):
        return {"status": "error", "message": "Invalid domain. Use: tech, finance, sports"}
    try:
        articles = fetch_articles(domain)
        return {"status": "ok", "domain": domain, "count": len(articles), "articles": articles}
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "message": str(e)}


def _parse_digest(text: str) -> dict:
    result  = {}
    pattern = re.split(r"(🔥 Top Headlines|🧠 Tech|💰 Finance|⚽ Sports)", text)
    for i in range(1, len(pattern), 2):
        key     = pattern[i].strip()
        content = pattern[i + 1].strip() if i + 1 < len(pattern) else ""
        bullets = [
            b.lstrip("- ").strip()
            for b in content.splitlines()
            if b.strip().startswith("-")
        ]
        result[key] = bullets
    return result
```

### File: ingestion.py
```
import os
import requests
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
from datetime import datetime, timezone

NEWS_API_KEY = os.getenv("NEWS_API_KEY")
NEWS_API_URL = "https://newsapi.org/v2/top-headlines"

# RSS feed sources per domain (BBC, Reuters)
RSS_FEEDS = {
    "tech": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/news/technology/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/technologyNews",
    ],
    "finance": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/news/business/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/businessNews",
    ],
    "sports": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/sport/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/sportsNews",
    ],
}

NEWSAPI_CATEGORIES = {
    "tech":    "technology",
    "finance": "business",
    "sports":  "sports",
}


def fetch_articles(domain: str, page_size: int = 8) -> list[dict]:
    articles = []
    articles.extend(_fetch_rss(domain))
    articles.extend(_fetch_newsapi(domain, page_size))
    # deduplicate by title at ingestion level
    seen, unique = set(), []
    for a in articles:
        key = a["title"].lower().strip()
        if key not in seen:
            seen.add(key)
            unique.append(a)
    return unique


def _fetch_newsapi(domain: str, page_size: int) -> list[dict]:
    if not NEWS_API_KEY:
        return []
    try:
        params = {
            "apiKey":   NEWS_API_KEY,
            "language": "en",
            "pageSize": page_size,
            "category": NEWSAPI_CATEGORIES[domain],
        }
        resp = requests.get(NEWS_API_URL, params=params, timeout=10)
        resp.raise_for_status()
        raw_list = resp.json().get("articles", [])
        return [
            _normalize(
                title=a["title"],
                content=a.get("description") or a.get("content", ""),
                source=a.get("source", {}).get("name", "NewsAPI"),
                published_at=a.get("publishedAt", _now()),
                category_hint=domain,
            )
            for a in raw_list
            if a.get("title") and a.get("description")
        ]
    except Exception:
        return []


def _fetch_rss(domain: str) -> list[dict]:
    articles = []
    for url in RSS_FEEDS[domain]:
        try:
            resp = requests.get(url, timeout=10, headers={"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"})
            resp.raise_for_status()
            root = ET.fromstring(resp.content)
            for item in root.findall(".//item")[:8]:
                title   = item.findtext("title", "").strip()
                content = item.findtext("description", "").strip()
                source  = item.findtext("source", url.split("/")[2])
                pub     = item.findtext("pubDate", _now())
                if title and content:
                    articles.append(_normalize(title, content, source, pub, domain))
        except Exception:
            continue
    return articles


def _normalize(title: str, content: str, source: str, published_at: str, category_hint: str) -> dict:
    return

```
### File: orchestrator.py
```
import time
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed
from ingestion import fetch_articles
from agents import run_agent

DOMAINS  = ["tech", "finance", "sports"]
MAX_RETRIES = 2


def run_pipeline() -> list[dict]:
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=len(DOMAINS)) as executor:
        futures = {
            executor.submit(_fetch_and_run_with_retry, domain): domain
            for domain in DOMAINS
        }
        results = {}
        for future in as_completed(futures):
            domain = futures[future]
            try:
                results[domain] = future.result()
            except Exception as e:
                results[domain] = {
                    "domain":  domain,
                    "bullets": [f"Pipeline error: {e}"],
                    "summary": f"- Pipeline error: {e}",
                    "count":   0,
                }

    # return in consistent order
    return [results[d] for d in DOMAINS]


def _fetch_and_run_with_retry(domain: str) -> dict:
    last_error = None
    for attempt in range(1, MAX_RETRIES + 1):
        try:
            articles = fetch_articles(domain)
            return run_agent(domain, articles)
        except Exception as e:
            last_error = e
            if attempt < MAX_RETRIES:
                time.sleep(2 ** attempt)  # exponential backoff
    raise last_error
```

### File: README.md
```
# 📡 AI News Digest — Multi-Agent News Pipeline

AI News Digest is an intelligent news briefing system powered by a multi-agent AI pipeline. It automatically collects real-time news from RSS feeds (BBC, Reuters) and NewsAPI across three domains — Technology, Finance, and Sports — then routes each domain through a specialized AI agent that filters, deduplicates, and summarizes the articles. A final Summary Agent merges all outputs, ranks the top stories by global impact, and delivers a clean daily briefing through a modern web dashboard.

## Tech Stack

| Layer | Technology |
|---|---|
| Backend | FastAPI, Uvicorn |
| LLM | LLaMA 3.3 70B via Groq (free) |
| News Sources | NewsAPI, BBC RSS, Reuters RSS |
| Agent Pipeline | Custom multi-agent (Filter → Chunk → Summarize → Deduplicate → Output) |
| Frontend | HTML, CSS, JavaScript |

## Setup

1. Clone the repo
   ```bash
   git clone https://github.com/rbbhadiyar/AI-News-Digest.git
   cd AI-News-Digest
   ```

2. Install dependencies
   ```bash
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

3. Create `.env` from the example
   ```bash
   cp .env.example .env
   ```
   Fill in your API keys inside `.env`:
   - **GROQ_API_KEY** → [console.groq.com](https://console.groq.com) (free)
   - **NEWS_API_KEY** → [newsapi.org](https://newsapi.org) (free tier)

4. Run
   ```bash
   python main.py
   ```

5. Open [http://localhost:8000](http://localhost:8000)

---

```
### File: summary_agent.py
```
import os
from groq import Groq

client = Groq(api_key=os.getenv("GROQ_API_KEY"))
MODEL = "llama-3.3-70b-versatile"

SYSTEM_PROMPT = """You are a Chief News Editor producing a daily briefing.

You receive bullet-point summaries from three specialist analysts: Tech, Finance, and Sports.

Your tasks:
1. Top Headlines: Pick the 3 most globally important stories across ALL domains. Rank by real-world impact.
2. Remove redundancy: If the same story appears in multiple sections, keep it only in Top Headlines.
3. Present each domain section cleanly with the bullets provided, removing any duplicates.
4. Keep each bullet concise (one sentence max).

Output STRICTLY in this format (use these exact emoji headers):

🔥 Top Headlines
- <most important story>
- <second most important>
- <third most important>

🧠 Tech
- <bullet>
- <bullet>

💰 Finance
- <bullet>
- <bullet>

⚽ Sports
- <bullet>
- <bullet>"""

DOMAIN_LABELS = {
    "tech":    "🧠 Tech",
    "finance": "💰 Finance",
    "sports":  "⚽ Sports",
}


def build_digest(agent_outputs: list[dict]) -> str:
    combined = "\n\n".join(
        f"{DOMAIN_LABELS.get(o['domain'], o['domain'])}:\n{o['summary']}"
        for o in agent_outputs
    )

    response = client.chat.completions.create(
        model=MODEL,
        messages=[
            {"role": "system", "content": SYSTEM_PROMPT},
            {"role": "user",   "content": combined},
        ],
        temperature=0.2,
    )

    return response.choices[0].message.content.strip()

```", agent="Code Analyst", status="completed", output="### File: agents.py
### File: app.py
```
from dotenv import load_dotenv
load_dotenv()

import re
from fastapi import FastAPI
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.staticfiles import StaticFiles
from fastapi.responses import FileResponse
from orchestrator import run_pipeline
from summary_agent import build_digest
from ingestion import fetch_articles

app = FastAPI()

app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=["*"],
    allow_methods=["GET"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

app.mount("/assets", StaticFiles(directory="frontend"), name="static")


@app.get("/")
def index():
    return FileResponse("frontend/index.html")


@app.get("/api/digest")
def get_digest():
    try:
        outputs = run_pipeline()
        digest  = build_digest(outputs)
        return {
            "status":   "ok",
            "sections": _parse_digest(digest),
            "raw":      digest,
            "agents":   [
                {"domain": o["domain"], "count": o["count"], "bullets": o["bullets"]}
                for o in outputs
            ],
        }
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "message": str(e)}


@app.get("/api/articles/{domain}")
def get_articles(domain: str):
    if domain not in ("tech", "finance", "sports"):
        return {"status": "error", "message": "Invalid domain. Use: tech, finance, sports"}
    try:
        articles = fetch_articles(domain)
        return {"status": "ok", "domain": domain, "count": len(articles), "articles": articles}
    except Exception as e:
        return {"status": "error", "message": str(e)}


def _parse_digest(text: str) -> dict:
    result  = {}
    pattern = re.split(r"(🔥 Top Headlines|🧠 Tech|💰 Finance|⚽ Sports)", text)
    for i in range(1, len(pattern), 2):
        key     = pattern[i].strip()
        content = pattern[i + 1].strip() if i + 1 < len(pattern) else ""
        bullets = [
            b.lstrip("- ").strip()
            for b in content.splitlines()
            if b.strip().startswith("-")
        ]
        result[key] = bullets
    return result
```

### File: ingestion.py
```
import os
import requests
import xml.etree.ElementTree as ET
from datetime import datetime, timezone

NEWS_API_KEY = os.getenv("NEWS_API_KEY")
NEWS_API_URL = "https://newsapi.org/v2/top-headlines"

# RSS feed sources per domain (BBC, Reuters)
RSS_FEEDS = {
    "tech": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/news/technology/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/technologyNews",
    ],
    "finance": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/news/business/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/businessNews",
    ],
    "sports": [
        "http://feeds.bbci.co.uk/sport/rss.xml",
        "https://feeds.reuters.com/reuters/sportsNews",
    ],
}

NEWSAPI_CATEGORIES = {
    "tech":    "technology",
    "finance": "business",
    "sports":  "sports",
}


def fetch_articles(domain: str, page_size: int = 8) -> list[dict]:
    articles = []
    articles.extend(_fetch_rss(domain))
    articles.extend(_fetch_newsapi(domain, page_size))
    # deduplicate by title at ingestion level
    seen, unique = set(), []
    for a in articles:
        key = a["title"].lower().strip()
        if key not in seen:
            seen.add(key)
            unique.append(a)
    return unique


def _fetch_newsapi(domain: str, page_size: int) -> list[dict]:
    if not NEWS_API_KEY:
        return []
    try:
        params = {
            "apiKey":   NEWS_API_KEY,
            "language": "en",
            "pageSize": page_size,
            "category": NEWSAPI_CATEGORIES[domain],
        }
        resp = requests.get(NEWS_API_URL, params=params, timeout=10)
        resp.raise_for_status()
        raw_list = resp.json().get("articles", [])
        return [
            _normalize(
                title=a["title"],
                content=a.get("description") or a.get("content", ""),
                source=a.get("source", {}).get("name", "NewsAPI"),
                published_at=a.get("publishedAt", _now()),
                category_hint=domain,
            )
            for a in raw_list
            if a.get("title") and a.get("description")
        ]
    except Exception:
        return []


def _fetch_rss(domain: str) -> list[dict]:
    articles = []
    for url in RSS_FEEDS[domain]:
        try:
            resp = requests.get(url, timeout=10, headers={"User-Agent": "Mozilla/5.0"})
            resp.raise_for_status()
            root = ET.fromstring(resp.content)
            for item in root.findall(".//item")[:8]:
                title   = item.findtext("title", "").strip()
                content = item.findtext("description", "").strip()
                source  = item.findtext("source", url.split("/")[2])
                pub     = item.findtext("pubDate", _now())
                if title and content:
                    articles.append(_normalize(title, content, source, pub, domain))
        except Exception:
            continue
    return articles


def _normalize(title: str, content: str, source: str, published_at: str, category_hint: str) -> dict:
    return

```
### File: orchestrator.py
```
import time
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed
from ingestion import fetch_articles
from agents import run_agent

DOMAINS  = ["tech", "finance", "sports"]
MAX_RETRIES = 2


def run_pipeline() -> list[dict]:
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=len(DOMAINS)) as executor:
        futures = {
            executor.submit(_fetch_and_run_with_retry, domain): domain
            for domain in DOMAINS
        }
        results = {}
        for future in as_completed(futures):
            domain = futures[future]
            try:
                results[domain] = future.result()
            except Exception as e:
                results[domain] = {
                    "domain":  domain,
                    "bullets": [f"Pipeline error: {e}"],
                    "summary": f"- Pipeline error: {e}",
                    "count":   0,
                }

    # return in consistent order
    return [results[d] for d in DOMAINS]


def _fetch_and_run_with_retry(domain: str) -> dict:
    last_error = None
    for attempt in range(1, MAX_RETRIES + 1):
        try:
            articles = fetch_articles(domain)
            return run_agent(domain, articles)
        except Exception as e:
            last_error = e
            if attempt < MAX_RETRIES:
                time.sleep(2 ** attempt)  # exponential backoff
    raise last_error
```

### File: README.md
```
# 📡 AI News Digest — Multi-Agent News Pipeline

AI News Digest is an intelligent news briefing system powered by a multi-agent AI pipeline. It automatically collects real-time news from RSS feeds (BBC, Reuters) and NewsAPI across three domains — Technology, Finance, and Sports — then routes each domain through a specialized AI agent that filters, deduplicates, and summarizes the articles. A final Summary Agent merges all outputs, ranks the top stories by global impact, and delivers a clean daily briefing through a modern web dashboard.

## Tech Stack

| Layer | Technology |
|---|---|
| Backend | FastAPI, Uvicorn |
| LLM | LLaMA 3.3 70B via Groq (free) |
| News Sources | NewsAPI, BBC RSS, Reuters RSS |
| Agent Pipeline | Custom multi-agent (Filter → Chunk → Summarize → Deduplicate → Output) |
| Frontend | HTML, CSS, JavaScript |

## Setup

1. Clone the repo
   ```bash
   git clone https://github.com/rbbhadiyar/AI-News-Digest.git
   cd AI-News-Digest
   ```

2. Install dependencies
   ```bash
   pip install -r requirements.txt
   ```

3. Create `.env` from the example
   ```bash
   cp .env.example .env
   ```
   Fill in your API keys inside `.env`:
   - **GROQ_API_KEY** → [console.groq.com](https://console.groq.com) (free)
   - **NEWS_API_KEY** → [newsapi.org](https://newsapi.org) (free tier)

4. Run
   ```bash
   python main.py
   ```

5. Open [http://localhost:8000](http://localhost:8000)

---

```
### File: summary_agent.py
```
import os
from groq import Groq

client = Groq(api_key=os.getenv("GROQ_API_KEY"))
MODEL = "llama-3.3-70b-versatile"

SYSTEM_PROMPT = """You are a Chief News Editor producing a daily briefing.

You receive bullet-point summaries from three specialist analysts: Tech, Finance, and Sports.

Your tasks:
1. Top Headlines: Pick the 3 most globally important stories across ALL domains. Rank by real-world impact.
2. Remove redundancy: If the same story appears in multiple sections, keep it only in Top Headlines.
3. Present each domain section cleanly with the bullets provided, removing any duplicates.
4. Keep each bullet concise (one sentence max).

Output STRICTLY in this format (use these exact emoji headers):

🔥 Top Headlines
- <most important story>
- <second most important>
- <third most important>

🧠 Tech
- <bullet>
- <bullet>

💰 Finance
- <bullet>
- <bullet>

⚽ Sports
- <bullet>
- <bullet>"""

DOMAIN_LABELS = {
    "tech":    "🧠 Tech",
    "finance": "💰 Finance",
    "sports":  "⚽ Sports",
}


def build_digest(agent_outputs: list[dict]) -> str:
    combined = "\n\n".join(
        f"{DOMAIN_LABELS.get(o['domain'], o['domain'])}:\n{o['summary']}"
        for o in agent_outputs
    )

    response = client.chat.completions.create(
        model=MODEL,
        messages=[
            {"role": "system", "content": SYSTEM_PROMPT},

const SECTIONS_META = {
  "🔥 Top Headlines": { icon: "🔥", badge: "HOT",     badgeClass: "badge-hot",     cardClass: "card-top" },
  "🧠 Tech":          { icon: "🧠", badge: "TECH",    badgeClass: "badge-tech",    cardClass: "" },
  "💰 Finance":       { icon: "💰", badge: "FINANCE", badgeClass: "badge-finance", cardClass: "" },
  "⚽ Sports":        { icon: "⚽", badge: "SPORTS",  badgeClass: "badge-sports",  cardClass: "" },
};

function setLoading(on) {
  const btn = document.getElementById("refresh-btn");
  const bar = document.getElementById("status-bar");
  btn.disabled = on;
  document.getElementById("btn-icon").textContent = on ? "⏳" : "⚡";
  bar.classList.toggle("visible", on);
}

function showError(msg) {
  const box = document.getElementById("error-box");
  box.textContent = "⚠️ " + msg;
  box.classList.add("visible");
}

function clearError() {
  document.getElementById("error-box").classList.remove("visible");
}

function renderSkeletons() {
  const grid = document.getElementById("digest-grid");
  grid.innerHTML = Array.from({ length: 4 }, () => `
    <div class="skeleton-card">
      <div class="skeleton-line short" style="margin-bottom:18px"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line long"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line medium"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line long"></div>
      <div class="skeleton-line medium"></div>
    </div>
  `).join("");
}

function renderDigest(sections) {
  const grid = document.getElementById("digest-grid");
  grid.innerHTML = "";

  const order = ["🔥 Top Headlines", "🧠 Tech", "💰 Finance", "⚽ Sports"];

  order.forEach(key => {
    const bullets = sections[key];
    if (!bullets || bullets.length === 0) return;

    const meta = SECTIONS_META[key] || { icon: "📰", badge: key, badgeClass: "", cardClass: "" };
    const li = bullets.map(b => `<li>${b}</li>`).join("");

    const card = document.createElement("div");
    card.className = `card ${meta.cardClass}`;
    card.innerHTML = `
      <div class="card-header">
        <span class="card-icon">${meta.icon}</span>
        <span class="card-title">${key}</span>
        <span class="card-badge ${meta.badgeClass}">${meta.badge}</span>
      </div>
      <ul class="bullet-list">${li}</ul>
    `;
    grid.appendChild(card);
  });

  document.getElementById("last-updated").textContent =
    "Last updated: " + new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
}

async function loadDigest() {
  clearError();
  setLoading(true);
  renderSkeletons();

  try {
    const res = await fetch("/api/digest");
    const data = await res.json();

    if (data.status === "error") {
      showError(data.message);
      document.getElementById("digest-grid").innerHTML = "";
      return;
    }

    renderDigest(data.sections);
  } catch (e) {
    showError("Could not reach the server. Make sure the backend is running.");
    document.getElementById("digest-grid").innerHTML = "";
  } finally {
    setLoading(false);
  }
}
